<div style="position:absolute;left:309.65px;top:435.91px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Assyrian Captivity</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:72.02px;top:451.87px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Amon (642-640)</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:72.02px;top:467.95px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Josiah (640-609)</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:72.02px;top:484.03px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Jehoahaz (609)</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:72.02px;top:499.99px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Jehoiakim (609-598)</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:72.02px;top:516.07px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Jehoiachim (598)</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:72.02px;top:532.03px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Zedekiah (598-587)</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:72.02px;top:548.11px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:72.02px;top:564.07px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Babylonian Captivity</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:300.53px;top:704.98px" class="cls_002"><span class="cls_002">19</span></div>
</div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:50%;margin-left:-306px;top:15238px;width:612px;height:792px;border-style:outset;overflow:hidden">
<div style="position:absolute;left:0px;top:0px">
<img src="5fb2c2c4-5f39-11ea-8b25-0cc47a792c0a_id_5fb2c2c4-5f39-11ea-8b25-0cc47a792c0a_files/background020.jpg" width=612 height=792></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:220.01px;top:70.20px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">From Davidic to Divided Kingdom</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:36.00px;top:86.30px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Ruler in Judah (South)</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:310.61px;top:86.30px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Ruler in Israel (North)</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:309.65px;top:100.22px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">0927 Jeroboam (927-906) fortifies Shechem, rejects the</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:318.65px;top:114.26px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Royal Zion Theology of the Davidic line designated</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:318.65px;top:128.30px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">by prophets, rejects the Jerusalem priesthood by</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:318.65px;top:142.34px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">appointing Aaronite non-Zadokite priests, institutes a</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:318.65px;top:156.38px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">new cultic calendar, and has annual celebrations at</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:318.65px;top:170.42px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Bethel  (he too ignores the Elide sanctuary at Shiloh),</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:318.65px;top:184.46px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">not Jerusalem. Israel in the north, desirous of retaining</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:318.65px;top:198.50px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">its traditions, locates its capital at Samaria.  Having a</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:318.65px;top:212.54px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">broadly diverse population on the main Syro-</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:318.65px;top:226.58px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Palestinian trade route and thus subject to outside</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:318.65px;top:240.50px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">influences, Jeroboam allows worship of Baal, largely to</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:318.65px;top:254.57px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">accommodate outsiders; he also builds sanctuaries at</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:318.65px;top:268.61px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Bethel and Dan with golden calves made to the</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:318.65px;top:282.65px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">specifications of Aaron’s golden calf to mark the</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:318.65px;top:296.69px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">borders. Israelite political life is, however, very</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:318.65px;top:310.73px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">unstable: seven kings are assassinated, each time with a</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:318.65px;top:324.77px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">regime change; only the lines of Omri and Jehu are able</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:318.65px;top:338.81px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">to hold kingship more than two generations.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:36.00px;top:352.85px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">0926 Rehoboam - In Judah, Rehoboam (926-910), whose mother, Naamah of Ammon, was one of Solomon’s</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:366.77px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">foreign wives, enjoys a 17-year reign. He retains Jerusalem as Judah's capital but in the fifth year of his reign (922),</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:380.81px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Egyptian pharaoh Shishaq captures all of the fortified towns leading to Jerusalem between Gezer and Gibeon.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:394.85px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">When he lays siege to Jerusalem, Rehoboam gives Shishaq all the treasures out of the temple as a tribute. The</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:408.89px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Egyptian campaign cuts off trade with south Arabia via Elath and the Negev established during Solomon's reign,</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:422.95px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">and Judah becomes a vassal state of Egypt. Of course, the priests attribute Shishaq’s invasion to “divine</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:436.99px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">punishment” for Rehoboam’s apostasy (disobedience to the priests).  “Judah did what was evil in the sight of the</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:451.03px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Lord, and they provoked him to jealousy with their sins which they committed, more than all that their fathers had</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:465.07px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">done. For they also built for themselves high places (altars to Baal), and pillars, and Asherim on every high hill and</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:479.11px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">under every green tree; and there were also male cult prostitutes in the land. They did according to all the</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:493.15px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">abominations of the nations which the Lord drove out before the people of Israel.” (1Kings 14:22-24) Chron’s</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:507.07px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">agenda here becomes plain: sin brings judgment, obedience brings blessing, and repentance brings deliverance.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:521.11px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">References in Chron to the north (Israel) are omitted whenever possible. Kings obedient to the priesthood</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:535.15px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">prosper in terms of military victory and wealth through tribute, building projects, rest, and progeny. Disobedient</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:549.19px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">kings experience punishment in the form of military defeat, physical deformity, illness, or untimely death.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:36.00px;top:563.23px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">0915 Abijah - Chron approves of the obedient Abijah  (though he is condemned in 1K 15:3), whose speech is a list of</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:577.27px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Chron's themes: David's throne, Solomon's temple, all Israel, and reliance upon God.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:36.00px;top:591.31px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">0913 Asa - Chron explains Asa’s foreign alliance with Ben-Hadad of Damascus and his diseased feet by dividing Asa</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:605.38px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">into two periods: one of faithfulness and a second of apostasy.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:288.05px;top:619.42px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">0879 Omri - (879-869) Israel reaches its zenith: when</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:633.34px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Israelite king Elah is assassinated by Zimri, Omri’s troops proclaim Omri king (nothing is said of his tribe), and he</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:647.38px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">builds a new capital at Samaria, he marries Jezebel, princess of Sidon, to his son, Ahab. Judah becomes a vassal to the</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:661.42px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Omrides (1Kgs 22:4). Epigraphical evidence of the Omride Dynasty includes the Mesha Inscription (the Moabite</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:675.46px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Stone, which relates how the Moabite god Chemosh, angry with his people, delivers them into the hands of Israel,</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:300.53px;top:704.98px" class="cls_002"><span class="cls_002">20</span></div>
</div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:50%;margin-left:-306px;top:16040px;width:612px;height:792px;border-style:outset;overflow:hidden">
<div style="position:absolute;left:0px;top:0px">
<img src="5fb2c2c4-5f39-11ea-8b25-0cc47a792c0a_id_5fb2c2c4-5f39-11ea-8b25-0cc47a792c0a_files/background021.jpg" width=612 height=792></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:31.20px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">then assists Mesha to liberate Moab). Jehoram of Israel then marshals Judah to reimpose Israelite control (2K3:4-</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:45.24px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">28); the Tel Dan Stele, which details how Israelite king Jehoram was killed (probably by Hazael, the Aramaean</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:59.28px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">king of Syria); and the Siloam Inscription, which commemorates the completion of a tunnel from Gihon Spring to</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:73.34px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Siloam Pool. Judah is not documented as a separate state until 733, when Ahaz severs his loyalty to Samaria. Omri</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:87.38px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">subjugates Moab, joins the anti-Assyrian coalition with Syria, reaches the Mediterranean, and allies with Tyre.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:36.00px;top:101.30px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">0873 Jehoshaphat (870-849) undertakes a maritime venture with Israel because access had been gained to the Gulf of</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:115.34px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Aqabah. His portrayal in Kings as the nadir of Judean fortunes is starkly different from that in Chron, to whom he</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:129.38px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">is so dear for removing the idols that Chron reads back into Jehoshaphat’s legend the post-exilic separation of civil</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:143.42px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">and sacred law. Chapter 20’s battle account is another roll call of Chron’s themes: Zadokite leadership, retributive</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:157.46px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">justice, reliance upon God, condemnation of foreign alliances, God's rule, and answered prayer.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:309.65px;top:171.50px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">0868 Ahab (868-850) associates with Phoenicians,</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:318.65px;top:185.54px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">marries Jezebel, builds a temple to Baal, and, worst of</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:318.65px;top:199.58px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">all, expropriates farmers - becoming thereby very</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:318.65px;top:213.62px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">unpopular. The Omride dynasty gains a reputation for</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:318.65px;top:227.66px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">economic and social injustice (Naboth Vineyard). The</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:318.65px;top:241.58px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">cities - Shechem and Samaria are prosperous and</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:318.65px;top:255.65px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">inclusive (Liberal), but the countryside is poor and</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:318.65px;top:269.69px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Yahwist (Fundamentalist). Yahwist prophets’</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:318.65px;top:283.73px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">condemnation of the apostasy of Israel and Jezebel is</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:318.65px;top:297.77px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">clearly the work of later pro-Judean compilers who,</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:318.65px;top:311.81px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">oversimplifying and exaggerating, project exclusive</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:318.65px;top:325.85px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Yahwism and the primacy of Jerusalem back into earlier</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:318.65px;top:339.89px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">times.  Foreign wives are the supposed source of palace</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:318.65px;top:353.93px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">apostasy. The Samarian temple to Baal provides</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:318.65px;top:367.85px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">foreign traders and diplomats a place to worship, but is</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:318.65px;top:381.89px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">a source of competition with exclusive Yahwism, and</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:318.65px;top:395.93px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">so must be shunned.  Elijah incites the crowd to murder</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:73.82px;top:408.89px" class="cls_008"><span class="cls_008">The Seductress Jezebel (or Cleopatra?)</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:318.65px;top:409.97px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">the prophets of Baal (1Kgs 18:40). Ahab is a co-leader</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:424.03px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">of the anti-Assyrian coalition. The names of Judah and Edom are absent from the list of supporters (perhaps they</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:438.07px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">were subsumed under Israel at the time). There are no archeological remains from the (supposedly grand)</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:452.11px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Solomonic Jerusalem to equal Ahab’s temple to Baal, or the fortifications of Megiddo, Jezreel, or Hazor.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:36.00px;top:466.15px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">~0850 Prophetic narratives in conflict: In the Elijah</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:480.19px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">stories: (Widow of Zarephath, The Challenge to Baal,</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:494.23px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Mount Horeb, The Vineyard of Naboth, Ahaziah,</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:508.15px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Ascension into Heaven, Elijah as a harbinger of the</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:522.19px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Messiah in Malachi), Israel is supreme, Baal worship is</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:536.23px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">widespread, Jezebel is the chief villain, and there is</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:550.27px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">conflict with Yahwist prophets. In the Elisha stories</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:564.31px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">(Adoption by Elijah, Elijah’s Ascension, Defeating the</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:578.35px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Moabites, Killing the Mocking Children, Multiplying</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:592.42px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">the Widow’s Oil, Resurrection of the Child of Shunem,</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:606.46px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Healing of the Syrian Naaman, Making Iron Float),</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:620.50px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Israel is weak, Yahwism is strongly supported, Israel is</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:634.42px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">on good terms with Yahwist prophets, and miraculous</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:648.46px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">deeds are performed.  The Ben-Hadad stories (three</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:662.50px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">battles between Syria and Israel) are expanded to give</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:676.54px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Yahwist prophets center stage, and emphasize</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:349.51px;top:687.70px" class="cls_009"><span class="cls_009">Elijah resurrects the son of the Widow of Zarephath</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:690.58px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Jehoshaphat’s loyalty to YHWH.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:301.49px;top:714.10px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">21</span></div>
</div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:50%;margin-left:-306px;top:16842px;width:612px;height:792px;border-style:outset;overflow:hidden">
<div style="position:absolute;left:0px;top:0px">
<img src="5fb2c2c4-5f39-11ea-8b25-0cc47a792c0a_id_5fb2c2c4-5f39-11ea-8b25-0cc47a792c0a_files/background022.jpg" width=612 height=792></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:324.05px;top:31.20px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">0850 Ahaziah (of Israel) (850-849) Ahab is</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:45.24px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">succeeded by his son Ahaziah, who is refused participation in Jehoshaphat’s maritime venture.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:36.00px;top:59.28px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">0849 Jehoram (849-842)  Ahaziah (of Israel) dies childless, so Ahab’s sister Athaliah marries Jehoram, son of</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:73.34px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Jehoshaphat, the two royal families are joined, and Israel and Judah reunite! This is, however, a period of rapid</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:87.38px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">decline for both kingdoms. Jehoram’s Moabite Campaign is retold to give center stage to Elisha, and again</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:101.30px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">emphasize Jehoshaphat’s piety - folk themes with numerous miraculous circumstances, which are ignored in Chron,</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:115.34px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">except to treat of Jehoshaphat, and blame the failure of his maritime venture on cooperation with Israel. Chron</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:129.38px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">deems Jehoram's alliance with Ahab in the north as responsible for his defeat in war, plague, and early death, all</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:143.42px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">which extend into the reigns of Ahaziah and Athaliah. All three are related to Ahab, adopt Ahabic Baalism, die</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:157.46px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">horrible deaths, and are denied burial in the royal cemetery.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:36.00px;top:171.50px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">0842 Ahaziah (of Judah) is a pawn of his mother, Athaliah, daughter of Ahab and Jezebel and granddaughter of</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:185.54px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Omri. He is killed either by Jehu (G2K) or Hazael (Tel Dan Stele).</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:36.00px;top:199.58px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">0842 Athaliah is the only non-Davidic ruler, woman,</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:213.62px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">and foreigner to sit upon Judah’s throne. Wife of King</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:227.66px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Jehoram through a foreign alliance with her father King</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:241.58px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Ahab of Israel, she takes the throne upon the death of</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:255.65px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">her son Ahaziah, and consolidates her power by</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:269.69px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">assassinating the remaining members of the Davidic</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:283.73px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">line. However, Jehoshabeath, Jehoram's daughter,</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:297.77px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">rescues her infant nephew Joash and hides him in the</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:311.81px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">temple for six years with her husband Jehoiada the</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:325.85px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">priest, thus preserving the Davidic line.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:36.00px;top:339.89px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">0842 Joash, under the tutelage of Jehoiada the priest,</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:353.93px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">carries out needed temple repairs, but after Jehoiada’s</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:367.85px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">death, Joash lapses into apostasy (contrary to 2K12) and</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:381.89px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">is assassinated in his bed by his servants, a victim of</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:425.71px;top:386.69px" class="cls_008"><span class="cls_008">Athaliah</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:395.93px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Chron's idea of retributive justice.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:324.05px;top:411.89px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">0839 Jehu  (839-822)  The Jehu Dynasty:  According</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:425.95px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">to G2K, Jehu, urged on by the prophet Elisha, kills Jehoram and Jezebel, then hosts a “feast” for the prophets of</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:439.99px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Baal whereat he massacres them, though in the Tel Dan Stele Hazael of Syria claims to have killed Jehoram and</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:454.03px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Ahaziah (of Judah), so that both Jehu in Samaria and Athaliah in Jerusalem seem to have come to power in the</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:468.07px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">political upheaval caused by Hazael.  Assyria then becomes active again and saves both Israel and Judah from further</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:482.11px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">attacks by Hazael. A problem for the compilers is that YHWH is expected to give victory to those that support</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:496.15px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">him, but Jehu was powerless before Hazael, and Jeroboam II overshadows his Yahwist Judean contemporary</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:510.19px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Uzziah. Furthermore, the Elisha stories from the Omride period fit the Jehu period better.  Chronicles, on the</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:524.11px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">other hand, completely ignores Israel, gives Levites important roles, and praises pro-Yahwist kings. The prophets</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:538.15px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Hosea and Amos emerge. During the Jehu Century, Israel and Judah submit to Syria and Assyria (according to the</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:552.19px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Black Obelisk).</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:36.00px;top:566.23px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">0800 Amaziah also starts off well, but sinks into apostasy (again contrary to 2 Kings 14) by rejecting the word of the</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:580.27px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">prophet, and suffers military defeat and assassination. For Chron, defeat proves guilt.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:324.05px;top:594.34px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">0788 Jeroboam II (788-748), restores Israel’s</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:608.38px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">borders and participates in the Assyrian economic realm, but as Assyria declines, the wealthy upper class of Israel</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:622.42px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">intensifies its predations on the weak.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:36.00px;top:636.46px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">0785 Uzziah (785-760) rules Judah under the shadow of Jeroboam II. He remains on good terms with the temple</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:650.50px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">priests for the first part of his reign, but Chron ascribes to him the cultic offense of burning incense (?), punished</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:664.42px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">by leprosy, banishment from the temple, and burial in a field. The prophet Amos is on the spot to point the finger</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:678.46px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">of blame.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:300.77px;top:714.10px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">22</span></div>
</div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:50%;margin-left:-306px;top:17644px;width:612px;height:792px;border-style:outset;overflow:hidden">
<div style="position:absolute;left:0px;top:0px">
<img src="5fb2c2c4-5f39-11ea-8b25-0cc47a792c0a_id_5fb2c2c4-5f39-11ea-8b25-0cc47a792c0a_files/background023.jpg" width=612 height=792></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:324.05px;top:31.20px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">0746 Zechariah - Shallum - Menahem (746-738)</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:45.24px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Zechariah is murdered by Shallum, a captain of his army, who takes the throne, thus ending the Jehu Dynasty.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:59.28px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Shallum is then deposed by Menahem, an ally of Assyria, now dominant under Tiglath-Pileser.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:36.00px;top:73.34px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">0742 Jotham is a refreshing model of obedience and blessing.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:36.00px;top:87.38px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">0735 Ahaz - Chron has Judah sinking to its lowest point</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:101.30px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">under Ahaz (according to G 2K, it was under</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:115.34px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Manasseh), because he worships foreign gods, and stops</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:129.38px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">the sacrifices in the temple. In Chron, bad kings (Ahaz,</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:143.42px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Manasseh) alternate with good kings (Hezekiah, Josiah).</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:157.46px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Ahaz sacrifices a son (2K16:3) to Moloch to lift the</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:171.50px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Syro-Ephraimite siege of Jerusalem, as had the Moabite</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:185.54px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">king Mesha on an earlier occasion. Ahaz, supervised by</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:199.58px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">the priest Uriah without protest (2K16:10), constructs</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:213.62px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">a Syrian altar, then is forced to abdicate because of health</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:227.66px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">(in Chron because he worships Syrian gods). Isaiah</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:241.58px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">encourages Ahaz to continue his pro-Assyrian policies,</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:255.65px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">but he is hard-pressed by Rezin of Syria, the Edomites,</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:269.69px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Israelite King Pekah, and the Philistines to join the anti-</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:384.79px;top:276.89px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Ahaz Sacrificing his Son</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:283.73px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Assyrian block (denounced by Micah). Isaiah supports</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:297.77px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">defending Jerusalem, and letting YHWH handle the rest. In 0 734, the Assyrians return to the relief of Judea, and</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:311.81px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">suppress Rezin. Ahaz, now independent of Israel, pays tribute to Tiglath-Pileser.0734 Pekah  (734-31) kills</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:325.85px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Pekakiah, and with support from Rezin, takes over part of Israel, now called Ephraim. To get Judah to join their</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:339.89px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">anti-Assyrian coalition, they then attack Jerusalem, as recorded in Isaiah 7-8. Pekah is killed, and Hoshea becomes</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:353.93px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">an Assyrian vassal.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:368.93px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">0732 Hoshea (732-722) Egypt’s 25</span><span class="cls_010">th</span><span class="cls_003"> Dynasty becomes a</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:382.97px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">competitor with Assyria for dominance in the Middle</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:397.01px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">East. Israelite King Hoshea buys in to the Egyptian</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:411.05px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">propaganda and ceases tribute payments to Assyria.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:424.99px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">When Assyria attacks Israel, the Egyptians do not come</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:439.03px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">to his aid, and Israel falls. G2K predictably blames</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:453.07px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Israel’s apostasy and failure to heed prophets for its fall.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:467.11px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Many people are deported from Israel to Assyria and</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:481.15px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">replaced with settlers from other parts of</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:495.19px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">the Assyrian empire - such population exchanges were</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:509.23px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">an established part of Assyrian imperial policy, a means</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:523.27px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">of breaking the old power structure. The captives in</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:537.31px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Assyria are split up, quickly assimilate, and thus ten</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:551.23px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">of the twelve tribes disappear.  Judah remains loyal to</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:411.91px;top:562.75px" class="cls_008"><span class="cls_008">Fall of Samaria</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:565.27px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Assyria (for the moment) and survives as an Assyrian</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:579.31px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">vassal.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:36.00px;top:593.38px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">0727 Hezekiah (727-699) Judah recovers with much biblical glorification in G2K and Isaiah. Samaria is taken by the</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:607.42px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Assyrians, and Isaiah advises Hezekiah, king of Judah in the South, to capitulate. The Assyrians surround</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:621.46px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Jerusalem, but are mysteriously killed (plague?), and Jerusalem is saved for now. Hezekiah shows the state</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:635.50px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">treasures to Merodach-baladan of Babylon, and Isaiah predicts he (Hezekiah) will be carried into Babylon.  In</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:649.54px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Chron, Levites purify the temple, reinstate proper worship, and destroy local shrines; the people bring tithes, and</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:663.58px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Hezekiah and Isaiah pray together. Hezekiah grows ill because of his pride, but humbles himself, and gets better;</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:677.50px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Jerusalem is spared. Back in the real world, Sargon dies, and revolt in Assyrian lands spreads. Isaiah: I told you that</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:691.54px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Assyria was a temporary power; Hezekiah revolts; Sennacherib invades and devastates the countryside, but can’t</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:301.37px;top:714.10px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">23</span></div>
</div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:50%;margin-left:-306px;top:18446px;width:612px;height:792px;border-style:outset;overflow:hidden">
<div style="position:absolute;left:0px;top:0px">
<img src="5fb2c2c4-5f39-11ea-8b25-0cc47a792c0a_id_5fb2c2c4-5f39-11ea-8b25-0cc47a792c0a_files/background024.jpg" width=612 height=792></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:31.20px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">take Jerusalem (partly due to the Siloam water tunnel). When Israel falls to Assyria (0722), Hezekiah invites the</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:45.24px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Northerners to a renewed celebration of the Passover, and, according to Chron, defends Jerusalem against</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:59.28px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Sennacherib's invading army through prayer. Overlooked by Chron are Hezekiah's surrender to Sennacherib, his</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:73.34px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">trust in foreign alliances, the stripping of the temple, and Isaiah's rebuke. Judah becomes an Assyrian client</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:87.38px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">state controlling the valuable olive industry.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:36.00px;top:101.30px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">0700 Universal dominion of YHWH  is asserted by Tobit, a Naphthalian captive in 722, who preaches that the</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:115.34px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">diaspora is good since it spreads worship of YHWH, and Isaiah who maintains YHWH has empowered the</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:129.38px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Assyrians and Babylonians in order to punish Israel. Isaiah also attacks corrupt officials who oppress the poor.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:36.00px;top:143.42px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">0698 Manasseh (698-644) is Judah's worst king, according to G2Kings: worse than Ahaz since he allowed non-</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:157.46px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Yahwist altars (as a quid pro quo for access to Assyria’s export markets?), though his reign of 55 years is the longest</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:171.50px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">in Israel or Judah. He inherits a war-torn country, yet with Assyrian power now at its acme, Judah prospers.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:36.00px;top:185.54px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">0642 Amon  undoes all the reforms of his repentant father, Manasseh. He is assassinated.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:36.00px;top:199.58px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">0641 Josiah (641-610) (8 years old) is put on the throne</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:213.62px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">by Judean aristocrats.  High priest Hilkiah “discovers”</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:227.66px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">the Book of Deuteronomy, which contains a</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:241.58px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">frightening assessment of the fate due to Judah for her</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:255.65px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">sins of tolerating other faiths. Josiah then murders all</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:269.69px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">agents of alien faiths (and sodomites) and destroys</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:283.73px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">their sanctuaries in a rampage that puts Kristallnacht to</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:297.77px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">shame. He reinstitutes Passover and then dies in an</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:311.81px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">encounter with Pharoah Neco. In Kings no mention is</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:325.85px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">made of a message from YHWH communicated by</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:339.89px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Neko (an odd choice for a messenger). The fact that in</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:353.93px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">spite of his pious actions, YHWH will still punish</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:367.85px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Judah for the sins of Manasseh indicates that the legend</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:381.89px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">was written after the fall of Judah. Further, the many</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:395.93px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">forms of non-Yahwist idolatry which he suppresses are</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:409.97px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">testimony to the continuous, widespread acceptance of</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:424.03px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Baal, Asherah and others in Judah in the 300 years since</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:372.31px;top:428.83px" class="cls_008"><span class="cls_008">Josiah Hearing the Book of the Law</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:439.99px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Solomon. Chron’s account of Josiah has the precocious child tearing down altars at twelve years of age, even before</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:454.03px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Deuteronomy is found. Pharaoh Neco arrives, having been sent by YHWH (?!), and warns Josiah to stay out of</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:468.07px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">his way. Neko fails to do so and is killed. Jeremiah makes a cameo appearance lamenting his death.0630 Assyrian</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:482.11px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">power collapses; now the competition is between Egypt and Babylonia</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:36.00px;top:496.15px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">0627-585 Jeremiah: ‘We should prosper in Babylon and</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:510.19px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">pray for local government while caring about</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:524.23px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Jerusalem.’</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:36.00px;top:538.27px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">0612 Period of Babylonian Domination - Babylonians</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:552.31px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">overrun the Assyrian capital, Nineveh.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:36.00px;top:566.23px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">0609 Pharoah Neco leads the Egyptian and Assyrian</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:580.27px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">armies out to confront the Babylonians; Josiah</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:594.34px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">inexplicably comes out to confront him and is killed at</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:608.38px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Megiddo.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:36.00px;top:622.42px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">0609 Jehoahaz-Jehoiakim - In the difficult geopolitical</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:636.46px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">situation that accompanied the decline of Assyrian</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:650.50px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">hegemony, Egypt and Babylon are both vying for</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:664.54px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">power. In 609 BCE, the Egyptians, hoping to bolster</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:678.58px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">the crumbling Assyrians in the face of Babylonian</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:378.07px;top:691.30px" class="cls_008"><span class="cls_008">Jeremiah, the Weeping Prophet</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:692.62px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">aggression, kill Josiah, depose his son Jehoahaz, and</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:299.81px;top:714.10px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">24</span></div>
</div>

<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:31.20px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">install Jehoiakim (608-598) as a puppet king. In 605, Nebuchadnezzar defeats Egypt at Carchemish and solidifies</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:45.24px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Babylon's supremacy. Jeremiah, supported by high-ranking family and officials, endorses submission to Babylon</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:59.28px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">and gives his famous temple sermon that the Jerusalem temple, like that of Shiloh, is to be destroyed. Jeremiah is</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:73.34px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">thereafter barred from entering the temple.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:36.00px;top:87.38px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">0598 An anti-Babylonian meeting, opposed by Jeremiah but supported by the people, is held in Jerusalem including</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:101.30px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Judah, Moab, Ammon, Tyre, and Sidon. Jehoiakim decides to withhold tribute from Babylon, and to ally with a</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:115.34px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">more assertive Egypt, though Pharoah Neco is only interested in access to the sea and will abandon Judah.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:129.38px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Nebuchadrezzar captures Jerusalem (the first time), as Jehoiakim dies waiting for Egyptian help.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:36.00px;top:143.42px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">0598 Jehoiachin - Zedekiah - Jehoiakim’s son Jehoiachin is captured and led to Babylon with Ezekiel and leading</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:157.46px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">citizens in the first Babylonian captivity. Zedekiah is placed on the throne by the Babylonians.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:309.65px;top:171.50px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">0587 Nebuchadrezzar has not been around for awhile,</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:318.65px;top:185.54px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">and Egypt defeats Nubia, so Zedekiah rebels.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:318.65px;top:199.58px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Jerusalem is besieged, and when Jeremiah predicts</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:318.65px;top:213.62px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">YHWH will fight for Babylon, he is put in the stocks.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:318.65px;top:227.66px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">This time, Egypt sends an army that briefly lifts the</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:318.65px;top:241.58px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">siege, but finally loses interest and the siege is</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:318.65px;top:255.65px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">reimposed. Zedekiah is taken before Nebuchadrezzar:</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:318.65px;top:269.69px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">his sons are killed before him, he is then blinded and</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:318.65px;top:283.73px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">taken to Babylon. Jerusalem is conquered (the second</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:318.65px;top:297.77px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">time) by Babylon, the Temple is destroyed, and</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:318.65px;top:311.81px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">leading families are forcibly moved to Babylon (Second</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:318.65px;top:325.85px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Babylonian Captivity). The destruction of Jerusalem,</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:318.65px;top:339.89px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">its Temple, and the Davidic dynasty by Babylon is</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:318.65px;top:353.93px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">deeply traumatic. Prophets and Deuteronomist priests</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:318.65px;top:367.85px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">will claim vindication of prophecies (to be written later</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:318.65px;top:381.89px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">in Babylon), and blame the fall of the state on apostasy</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:318.65px;top:395.93px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">rather than YHWH’s weakness. G2K is written to</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:318.65px;top:409.97px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">explain to a Judah in Babylon why they were exiled;</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:318.65px;top:424.03px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Chron is written to the returned community,</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:126.26px;top:435.91px" class="cls_008"><span class="cls_008">Babylonian Captivity</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:318.65px;top:438.07px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">explaining Jeremiah's announcement that the exile</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:70.94px;top:447.91px" class="cls_008"><span class="cls_008">Woodcut by Jost Amman, Nurenberg circa 1570</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:318.65px;top:452.11px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">would last seventy years, a mere interlude  to allow the</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:318.65px;top:466.15px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">land to enjoy its neglected Sabbaths.</span></div>

<div style="position:absolute;left:267.65px;top:32.16px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Babylonian Rule</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:36.00px;top:48.24px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">The reign of Gedaliah, a non-Davidic ruler appointed by Nebuchadrezzar, is suppressed by the biblical compilers.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:62.28px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Ishmael, a Davidic claimant, assassinates Gedaliah, but is opposed by Judean officials, and so flees to Egypt, taking</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:76.34px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Jeremiah. The third Babylonian deportation then ensues. G2K and Chron are silent as to Judah after the fall, but</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:90.38px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Jeremiah, Ezekiel and Deutero-Isaiah 40-55 document the state of affairs. Aramaic becomes the dominant spoken</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:104.30px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">language. Deutero-Isaiah asserts the first truly Hebrew monotheism by asserting that gods other than YHWH are</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:118.34px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">impotent idols;</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:36.00px;top:134.42px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">There is also an Egyptian diaspora: the Elephantine military colony assimilates with Egyptians, but keeps contact</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:148.46px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">with Jerusalem and Samaria, and has a temple for syncretic worship condemned by Jeremiah</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:281.93px;top:164.42px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">~~~~~~~~</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:251.57px;top:422.83px" class="cls_008"><span class="cls_008">Job Rebuked by his Friends</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:36.00px;top:436.15px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">0550 The Book of Job is written with its fascinating Theodice and portrayal of Satan as opposing counsel chatting</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:450.19px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">with the LORD and cajoling Him into destroying the life of Job.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:54.00px;top:467.83px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Evolution of Theodice: why do bad things happen to good people?</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:54.00px;top:483.79px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">1. Free will - It’s not God's fault; you somehow deserve it.  Asked why God allows cruelty against children,</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:63.00px;top:497.83px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Pope Francis responded that people have free will; interestingly, the abuser has free will, not the abused.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:54.00px;top:513.79px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">2. Redemptive - God tests us to find the limits of our faith.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:54.00px;top:529.87px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">3. Mystery - It's all part of the plan that you can’t understand.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:54.00px;top:545.83px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">4. Divine love - God punishes those he loves. (My favorite)</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:54.00px;top:561.91px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">5. Deuteronomistic - Group punishment for the sin of one/a few; namely, the failure of a ruler to obey</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:63.00px;top:575.95px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">God (as interpreted by priests) - a theory devised by … priests!</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:54.00px;top:591.94px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">6. Apocalyptic - The Zoroastrian (Persian) idea that the world is dualistic - either good or evil - and that</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:63.00px;top:605.98px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">now, since no other theory seems valid, it is dominated by evil. But suffering will be vanquished at the</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:63.00px;top:620.02px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">end of time, when the Davidic Messiah will expel the strangers, resurrect the dead, reward the good,</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:63.00px;top:634.18px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">punish the evil, and rule in righteousness until Judgment Day. (Don’t hold your breath.)</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:286.37px;top:651.58px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">~~~~~~~~</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:300.05px;top:714.10px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">26</span></div>
</div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:50%;margin-left:-306px;top:20852px;width:612px;height:792px;border-style:outset;overflow:hidden">
<div style="position:absolute;left:0px;top:0px">
<img src="5fb2c2c4-5f39-11ea-8b25-0cc47a792c0a_id_5fb2c2c4-5f39-11ea-8b25-0cc47a792c0a_files/background027.jpg" width=612 height=792></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:271.61px;top:31.20px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">The Persian Era</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:36.00px;top:47.28px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">0539 Cyrus II captures Babylon - The Persian era will last until Alexander in 0332. Under Persia, the exiles are</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:61.20px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">allowed to return from Babylon, rebuild the temple with the Zadokite High Priest as ruler, though many exiles stay</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:75.26px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">in Babylon. The Persian era lays the foundations for the unified Judaic religion and the beginning of a scriptural</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:89.30px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">canon.  The Davidic Zerubbabel is appointed Governor of Yehud, exciting Messianic hopes. Zecheriah: ‘He is</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:103.34px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">chosen by god, redemption is imminent,’ and so he is relieved of his duties (and killed?) by the Persians.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:36.00px;top:119.42px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">0515 The </span><A HREF="https://en.m.wikipedia.org/wiki/Second_Temple_period">Second Temple is consecrated. The period</A><span class="cls_003"> is characterized by strict <A HREF="https://en.m.wikipedia.org/wiki/Monotheism">monotheism,</A> the emergence of beliefs</div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:133.46px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">regarding </span><A HREF="https://en.m.wikipedia.org/wiki/Angel">angels</A><span class="cls_003"> and <A HREF="https://en.m.wikipedia.org/wiki/Demon">demons,</A> and the increasingly important institution of the synagogue. Yehud becomes a</div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:147.38px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">theocracy ruled by hereditary high priests, with a Persian-appointed governor, frequently Jewish, charged with</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:161.42px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">keeping order and seeing that taxes are paid. The city is refortified, and Judean life is reformed. Biblical sources</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:175.46px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">focus almost exclusively on highly Yahwistic exilic returnees, with no information on returnees before Nehemiah:</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:189.50px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">it may have been more desirable to stay in Babylon, as Josephus relates, many were “unwilling to leave their</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:203.54px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">property.”</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:36.00px;top:219.62px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">0445 Nehemiah, Cupbearer to the Persian King, with</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:233.66px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">the status of a Persian royal governor, on the order of</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:247.61px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Artaxerxes executes Jewish law, rebuilds the walls of</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:261.65px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Jerusalem, and demands a pure genealogy from those</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:275.69px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">who wish to worship at the Temple. He brings strict</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:289.73px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Yahwism based on Deuteronomy, restores the Levites,</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:303.77px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">enforces the Sabbath, and demands that foreign wives</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:317.81px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">and children be sent away: Judaism is born, along with</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:331.85px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">the Samaritan schism. Nehemiah also alleviates the</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:345.89px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">exploitation of the poor, who were selling family</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:359.93px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">members into slavery and were paying usurious interest</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:373.85px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">on loans made contrary to the law, then he returns to</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:387.89px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Persian court to defend himself.These returnees,</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:401.93px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">though they waited nearly one hundred years to leave</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:415.97px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Babylon, bear great disdain for those who stayed in</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:430.03px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Yehud, based partly on the exclusivism that the exiles</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:444.07px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">developed while in Babylon and also partly on disputes</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:458.11px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">over property.  But wait! Didn’t Nehemiah rule after</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:472.15px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Ezra? Not according to the times in office of the high</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:486.19px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">priests: Eliashib under Nehemiah (Neh 3:1,20; 13:4),</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:341.69px;top:496.15px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Nehemiah Rebuilds the Walls of Jerusalem</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:500.23px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">and Jehohanan under Ezra (10:6).</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:36.00px;top:516.19px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">0407 Jews of Elephantine (Egypt) appeal for help rebuilding their temple, but are denied.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:36.00px;top:532.27px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">0398 Ezra, part of the Babylonian Revival, returns to Jerusalem, has the Torah read. Under Ezra, Judaism becomes</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:546.31px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">a religion of the book, with reading as important as sacrifice as an act of worship. Ezra may have been the first</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:560.23px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">‘rabbi,’ though he preached neither end of days, nor Davidic preference, nor blatant nationalism.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:36.00px;top:576.31px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">0350 Chron  rewrites Biblical stories strongly to David’s advantage.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:36.36px;top:592.42px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">0340  Samarian leader Sanbalat supports Alexander against Persia; Alexander is victorious, and so the Samaritan</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.36px;top:606.34px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Joseph tribes (Manassah, Ephraim) are allowed to build a Temple on Mt. Gorizim (Nablus). Greek culture</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.36px;top:620.38px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">spreads with Alexander’s victory over Persia.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:281.93px;top:636.46px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">~~~~~~~~</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:300.53px;top:714.10px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">27</span></div>
</div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:50%;margin-left:-306px;top:21654px;width:612px;height:792px;border-style:outset;overflow:hidden">
<div style="position:absolute;left:0px;top:0px">
<img src="5fb2c2c4-5f39-11ea-8b25-0cc47a792c0a_id_5fb2c2c4-5f39-11ea-8b25-0cc47a792c0a_files/background028.jpg" width=612 height=792></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:246.65px;top:31.20px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Alexander and Hellenism</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:36.00px;top:47.28px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">0332 </span><A HREF="https://en.m.wikipedia.org/wiki/Alexander_the_Great">Alexander the Great</A> conquers Persia. On Alexander’s death in 323, his general Seleucus takes the Fertile</div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:61.20px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Crescent, and Ptolemy takes Egypt. Similarities between Jesus and Alexander: divine adoption, dual divine-</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:75.26px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">human parentage, virgin birth, universal transformative mission, death at 33, deification.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:91.34px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Conquest of the Holy Land by yet another foreign power in spite of the piety of the state (barring foreign wives</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:105.38px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">and foreign gods), leads to a rejection of the Deuteronomist view and the emergence of Messianic Apocalypticism</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:119.42px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">in the prophet Daniel.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:234.53px;top:342.05px" class="cls_008"><span class="cls_008">Alexander in the Temple of Jerusalem</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:353.21px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Alexander brings a flood of new settlers into the area, creating a new political-social reality - Hellenism: Greek</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:367.25px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">becomes the lingua franca; a new scientific, literary and legal environment emerges; the personal philosophy of</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:381.29px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Stoicism helps individuals to cope with a confused social reality; religious syncretism becomes the basis of the</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:395.21px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">dominant common culture among the upper classes of these regions until Islam in the 7</span><span class="cls_010">th</span><span class="cls_003"> century CE. Universalism</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:409.25px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">(peaceful coexistence) is the new standard, but is emphatically rejected by Yahwistic Jews, who are portrayed by</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:423.31px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">the civilized world as misanthropic and inhumane. Jews’ refusal to worship the Emperor, and their habit of sending</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:437.35px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">money to Jerusalem mark them for suspicion as a fifth column.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:36.00px;top:453.43px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">0301 </span><A HREF="https://en.m.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ptolemy_I">Ptolemy I</A><span class="cls_003"> of Egypt takes Jerusalem (<A HREF="https://en.m.wikipedia.org/wiki/Yehud_Medinata">Yehud Medinata</A>) by attacking on the Sabbath.</div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:245.81px;top:633.70px" class="cls_008"><span class="cls_008">Maccabees oppose Antiochus IV</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:644.98px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">0300 Traditionalists vs. Hellenizers: A prolonged internal struggle begins, manifest early in disputes over the</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:658.90px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">calendar. The common core of Judaism is determined: God as an active element in history, the Torah, support for</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:672.94px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">the Temple, establishment of synagogues, dietary laws, circumcision, the Sabbath, exclusive Yahwism.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:286.37px;top:689.02px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">~~~~~~~~</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:300.41px;top:714.10px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">28</span></div>
</div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:50%;margin-left:-306px;top:22456px;width:612px;height:792px;border-style:outset;overflow:hidden">
<div style="position:absolute;left:0px;top:0px">
<img src="5fb2c2c4-5f39-11ea-8b25-0cc47a792c0a_id_5fb2c2c4-5f39-11ea-8b25-0cc47a792c0a_files/background029.jpg" width=612 height=792></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:251.69px;top:47.28px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Synagogues and Rabbis</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:36.00px;top:63.24px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">0250 1 Enoch is written, of which an Ethiopic text is later found at Qumran. Themes include for the first time many</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:77.30px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">of the accoutrements of later Christian belief: a solar calendar, angels, heaven and hell, Son of Man existent before</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:91.34px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">creation, judgment after death, resurrection of believers - ideas also reflected in Daniel 12:2.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:36.00px;top:107.30px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">0230 Synagogues: Though perhaps mentioned by Ezekiel “I will be a comfort to them,” and though Ezra led readings</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:121.34px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">of the Torah, congregational meetings are not regular until the first synagogue, most likely the proseuche - prayer</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:135.38px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">(venue) begun in Egypt during the reign of Ptolemy III, at which meetings there are a priest and an elder (rabbi),</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:149.42px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">where diaspora communities gather to read the Torah under a leader (Acts). Synagogues will not be introduced to</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:163.46px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Judea until 0070 CE. Access to God is no longer the exclusive prerogative of the priests.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:36.00px;top:179.54px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">0200 Sadducees (“descendants of Zadok”) believe that people have total free will, that there is no after life (like</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:193.58px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Epicureans, though here an outgrowth of the Zadokite teaching that one should serve God as though no wage -</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:207.50px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Heaven - were paid), that written tradition can come only from Moses, that ‘legitimate’ priests must take back</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:221.54px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">their rights from the Hasmoneans. Sadducees are, however, wealthy and alienated from the common people.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:36.00px;top:429.55px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">0200 Pharisees (Aramaic “separated ones”) believe that some things are determined by fate and others by will, so</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:443.59px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">divine reward/punishment are deserved since we are somewhat responsible. Why then is there no justice? There</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:457.63px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">must be justice in an afterworld - similar to Stoicism, and the oral tradition from Moses, the first “rabbi”; the</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:471.67px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">message attracts the lower classes (quite close to that of the Christians, so the conflict between Pharisees and</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:485.71px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Christians will be so bitter). Because of their affinity to the masses, they are authorized to determine Temple</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:499.63px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">practices for Sadducees.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:286.37px;top:515.71px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">~~~~~~~~</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:300.53px;top:714.10px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">29</span></div>
</div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:50%;margin-left:-306px;top:23258px;width:612px;height:792px;border-style:outset;overflow:hidden">
<div style="position:absolute;left:0px;top:0px">
<img src="5fb2c2c4-5f39-11ea-8b25-0cc47a792c0a_id_5fb2c2c4-5f39-11ea-8b25-0cc47a792c0a_files/background030.jpg" width=612 height=792></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:253.49px;top:31.20px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">The Septuagint (LXX)</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:36.00px;top:47.28px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Greek-speaking Jews need a translation of the Bible into Greek, the Septuagint, in which certain liberties are taken:</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:61.20px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">themes of the after-life are introduced; Proverbs is translated very freely; certain factual inconsistencies emerge:</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:75.26px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">the enemies of Israel, who had been Aramaeans and Philistines are now Syrians and coastal Greek cities; words</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:89.30px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">assume new meanings; there is a reluctance to refer to anthropomorphism - in Isaiah 38:11 ‘the Lord’ becomes</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:103.34px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">‘salvation,’ Exodus 24:10 ‘the Lord’ becomes ‘the place’; mistakes abound: Isaiah 7:14 ‘alma - young woman’</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:117.38px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">becomes ‘parthenos - virgin.’ This one error alone leads to millennia of creative theologizing). Some Jewish scholars</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:131.42px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">contend that only the Pentateuch is translated under divine guidance, hence only those translations are accurate.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:36.00px;top:317.09px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">One egregious example of rampant translation error is Isaiah Chapter Three, in which there are 41 translation errors.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:331.13px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">I have highlighted only a few verses below. My favorite is ‘transparent Spartan dresses’ for ‘crisping pins.’</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:347.21px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">The format below is:   Hebrew Masoretic Text, King James Version (generally correct),</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:153.02px;top:363.17px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Septuagint (often errant), Septuagint in English</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:260.45px;top:379.25px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Isaiah Chapter Three</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:223.73px;top:396.65px" class="cls_013"><span class="cls_013">םיˇחלהו ˇפנה יתבו םירשקהו תˣדעצהו םיראפה</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:557.98px;top:396.65px" class="cls_014"><span class="cls_014">כ</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:418.63px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003"> </span><A HREF="https://www.kingjamesbibleonline.org/Isaiah-3-20/">20</A> The bonnets, and the ornaments of the legs, and the headbands, and the tablets, and the earrings, (five items)</div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:436.15px" class="cls_007"><span class="cls_007">20 καὶ τὴν σύνθεσιν τοῦ κόσμου τῆς δόξης καὶ τοὺς χλιδῶνας, καὶ τὰ ψέλια καὶ τὸ ἐμπλόκιον καὶ τὰ περιδέξια</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:449.95px" class="cls_007"><span class="cls_007">καὶ τοὺς δακτυλίους καὶ τὰ ἐνώτια</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:45.00px;top:460.15px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">20 and the array of glorious ornaments, and the armlets, and the bracelets, and the wreathed work, and the finger-</span></div>
