<div style="position:absolute;left:222.41px;top:67.20px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Sermon on the Mount - Beatitudes (Q)</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:72.02px;top:83.30px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">[The New Testament unabashedly offers rewards for certain forms of conduct. Heaven as a reward for</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:97.22px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">virtuous behavior is a non-Jewish concept borrowed from Zoroastrianism along with dualistic</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:111.26px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">cosmology. ]</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:237.65px;top:385.13px" class="cls_008"><span class="cls_008">Basilica Papale di San Francesco Assissi</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:72.02px;top:398.45px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Mt 5:1 And seeing the multitudes, he went up into a mountain: and when he was set, his disciples came</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:412.49px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">unto him: 5:2 And he opened his mouth, and taught them, saying, 5:3 Blessed are the poor in spirit: for</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:426.55px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">theirs is the kingdom of heaven. 5:4 Blessed are they that mourn: for they shall be comforted. 5:5</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:440.59px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Blessed are the meek: for they shall inherit the earth. 5:6 Blessed are they which do hunger and thirst</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:454.63px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">after righteousness: for they shall be filled. 5:7 Blessed are the merciful: for they shall obtain mercy. 5:8</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:468.67px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Blessed are the pure in heart: for they shall see God. 5:9 Blessed are the peacemakers: for they shall be</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:482.71px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">called the children of God. 5:10 Blessed are they which are persecuted for righteousness' sake: for theirs</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:496.75px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">is the kingdom of heaven. 5:11 Blessed are ye, when men shall revile you, and persecute you, and shall</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:510.67px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">say all manner of evil against you falsely, for my sake. 5:12 Rejoice, and be exceeding glad: for great is</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:524.71px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">your reward in heaven: for so persecuted they the prophets which were before you.</span></div>

<div style="position:absolute;left:254.57px;top:67.20px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Turn the other cheek (Q)</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:72.02px;top:83.30px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">[Jesus emphasizes that followers should be concerned not with physical well-being, but with their spiritual</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:97.22px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">well-being. “Hate thine enemy” is inferred from commentary on post-Exilic dealings with Gentiles]</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:72.02px;top:403.25px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Mt 5:38 Ye have heard that it hath been said, An eye for an eye, and a tooth for a tooth: 5:39 But I say</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:417.29px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">unto you, That ye resist not evil: but whosoever shall smite thee on thy right cheek, turn to him the</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:431.35px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">other also. 5:40 And if any man will sue thee at the law, and take away thy coat, let him have thy cloak</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:445.39px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">also. 5:41  And whosoever shall compel thee to go a mile, go with him twain. 5:42 Give to him that</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:459.43px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">asketh thee, and from him that would borrow of thee turn not thou away. 5:43 Ye have heard that it</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:473.47px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">hath been said, Thou shalt love thy neighbour, and hate thine enemy. 5:44 But I say unto you, Love</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:487.39px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">your enemies, bless them that curse you, do good to them that hate you, and pray for them which</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:501.43px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">despitefully use you, and persecute you; 5:45 That ye may be the children of your Father which is in</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:515.47px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">heaven: for he maketh his sun to rise on the evil and on the good, and sendeth rain on the just and on the</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:529.51px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">unjust. 5:46 For if ye love them which love you, what reward have ye? do not even the publicans the</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:543.55px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">same?</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:117.70px;top:543.55px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">5:47 And if ye salute your brethren only, what do ye more than others? do not even the</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:557.59px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">publicans so?  5:48 Be ye therefore perfect, even as your Father which is in heaven is perfect.</span></div>

<div style="position:absolute;left:258.53px;top:67.20px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Hypocrites: Prayer (Q)</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:72.02px;top:83.30px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Mt 6:5 And when thou prayest, thou shalt not be as the hypocrites are: for they love to pray standing in</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:97.22px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">the synagogues and in the corners of the streets, that they may be seen of men. Verily I say unto you,</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:111.26px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">They have their reward. 6:6 But thou, when thou prayest, enter into thy closet, and when thou hast</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:354.41px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">shut thy door, pray to thy Father which is in secret; and thy Father which seeth in secret shall reward</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:368.45px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">thee openly. 6:7 But when ye pray, use not vain repetitions, as the heathen do: for they think that they</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:382.49px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">shall be heard for their much speaking. 6:8 Be not ye therefore like unto them: for your Father knoweth</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:396.53px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">what things ye have need of, before ye ask him. 6:9 After this manner therefore pray ye: Our Father</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:410.57px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">which art in heaven, Hallowed be thy name. 6:10 Thy kingdom come, Thy will be done in earth, as it is</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:424.63px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">in heaven. 6:11 Give us this day our daily bread. 6:12 And forgive us our debts, as we forgive our</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:438.67px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">debtors. 6:13 And lead us not into temptation, but deliver us from evil: For thine is the kingdom, and</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:452.59px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">the power, and the glory, for ever. Amen. 6:14 For if ye forgive men their trespasses, your heavenly</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:466.63px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Father will also forgive you: 6:15 But if ye forgive not men their trespasses, neither will your Father</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:480.67px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">forgive your trespasses.</span></div>

<div style="position:absolute;left:309.17px;top:699.70px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">79</span></div>

<div style="position:absolute;left:50%;margin-left:-306px;top:63358px;width:612px;height:792px;border-style:outset;overflow:hidden">
<div style="position:absolute;left:0px;top:0px">
<img src="5fb2c2c4-5f39-11ea-8b25-0cc47a792c0a_id_5fb2c2c4-5f39-11ea-8b25-0cc47a792c0a_files/background080.jpg" width=612 height=792></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:241.49px;top:67.20px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Hypocrites: God and Mammon</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:72.02px;top:83.30px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">How quickly money can ease the nagging conscience of churchmen who try to reconcile this Scripture with</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:97.22px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">the desire to befriend the wealthy! Jesus could not have been clearer in his condemnation of those who</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:111.26px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">“lay up treasures upon earth,” yet the rich and their collaborationist clergy have brazenly built their altar</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:125.30px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">to Mammon and his “Gospel of Wealth” in the very sepulcher of the church.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:99.02px;top:141.38px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Mt 6:19 Lay not up for yourselves treasures</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:108.02px;top:155.42px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">upon earth, where moth and rust doth</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:108.02px;top:169.46px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">corrupt, and where thieves break through</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:108.02px;top:183.38px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">and steal: 6:20 But lay up for yourselves</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:108.02px;top:197.42px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">treasures in heaven, where neither moth</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:108.02px;top:211.46px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">nor rust doth corrupt, and where thieves</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:108.02px;top:225.50px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">do not break through nor steal: 6:21 For</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:108.02px;top:239.54px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">where your treasure is, there will your</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:108.02px;top:253.61px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">heart be also. 6:22 The light of the body is</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:108.02px;top:267.65px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">the eye: if therefore thine eye be single, thy</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:108.02px;top:281.69px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">whole body shall be full of light. 6:23 But if</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:108.02px;top:295.73px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">thine eye be evil, thy whole body shall be</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:108.02px;top:309.77px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">full of darkness.  If therefore the light that</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:108.02px;top:323.69px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">is in thee be darkness, how great is that</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:108.02px;top:337.73px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">darkness!</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:163.32px;top:337.73px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">6:24 No man can serve two</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:108.02px;top:351.77px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">masters: for either he will hate the one, and</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:108.02px;top:365.81px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">love the other; or else he will hold to the one,</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:108.02px;top:379.85px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">and despise the other. Ye cannot serve</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:108.02px;top:395.93px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">God and mammon. 6:25 Therefore I say unto you, Take no thought for your life, what ye</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:108.02px;top:409.85px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">shall eat, or what ye shall drink; nor yet for your body, what ye shall put on. Is not the life</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:108.02px;top:423.91px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">more than meat, and the body than raiment?  6:26 Behold the fowls of the air: for they sow</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:108.02px;top:437.95px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">not, neither do they reap, nor gather into barns; yet your heavenly Father feedeth them. Are</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:108.02px;top:451.99px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">ye not much better than they?  6:27 Which of you by taking thought can add one cubit unto</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:108.02px;top:466.03px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">his stature?  6:28 And why take ye thought for raiment? Consider the lilies of the field, how</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:108.02px;top:480.07px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">they grow; they toil not, neither do they spin: 6:29 And yet I say unto you, That even</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:108.02px;top:494.11px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Solomon in all his glory was not arrayed like one of these. 6:30 Wherefore, if God so clothe</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:108.02px;top:508.15px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">the grass of the field, which to day is, and to morrow is cast into the oven, shall he not much</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:108.02px;top:522.19px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">more clothe you, O ye of little faith?  6:31 Therefore take no thought, saying, What shall we</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:108.02px;top:536.23px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">eat? or, What shall we drink? or, Wherewithal shall we be clothed?  6:32 (For after all these</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:108.02px;top:550.15px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">things do the Gentiles seek:) for your heavenly Father knoweth that ye have need of all these</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:108.02px;top:564.19px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">things. 6:33 But seek ye first the kingdom of God, and his righteousness; and all these things</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:108.02px;top:578.23px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">shall be added unto you. 6:34 Take therefore no thought for the morrow: for the morrow</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:108.02px;top:592.30px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">shall take thought for the things of itself. Sufficient unto the day is the evil thereof.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:293.93px;top:612.46px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">~~~~~~~</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:308.69px;top:699.70px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">80</span></div>
</div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:50%;margin-left:-306px;top:64160px;width:612px;height:792px;border-style:outset;overflow:hidden">
<div style="position:absolute;left:0px;top:0px">
<img src="5fb2c2c4-5f39-11ea-8b25-0cc47a792c0a_id_5fb2c2c4-5f39-11ea-8b25-0cc47a792c0a_files/background081.jpg" width=612 height=792></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:262.37px;top:67.20px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">The Golden Rule (Q)</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:72.02px;top:83.30px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">The criterion for salvation is clear: good fruit, i.e., good works. False prophets call upon Jesus’ name, but</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:97.22px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">do not perform his sayings.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:72.02px;top:366.29px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Mt 7:12 Therefore all things whatsoever ye would that men should do to you, do ye even so to them: for</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:380.33px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">this is the law and the prophets. 7:13 Enter ye in at the strait gate: for wide is the gate, and broad is the</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:394.37px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">way, that leadeth to destruction, and many there be which go in thereat: 7:14 Because strait is the gate,</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:408.41px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">and narrow is the way, which leadeth unto life, and few there be that find it. 7:15 Beware of false</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:422.47px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">prophets, which come to you in sheep's clothing, but inwardly they are ravening wolves. 7:16 Ye shall</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:436.51px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">know them by their fruits. Do men gather grapes of thorns, or figs of thistles?  7:17 Even so every good</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:450.55px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">tree bringeth forth good fruit; but a corrupt tree bringeth forth evil fruit. 7:18 A good tree cannot</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:464.59px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">bring forth evil fruit, neither can a corrupt tree bring forth good fruit. 7:19 Every tree that bringeth</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:478.51px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">not forth good fruit is hewn down, and cast into the fire. 7:20 Wherefore by their fruits ye shall know</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:492.55px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">them. 7:21 Not every one that saith unto me, Lord, Lord, shall enter into the kingdom of heaven; but</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:506.59px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">he that doeth the will of my Father which is in heaven. 7:22 Many will say to me in that day, Lord, Lord,</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:520.63px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">have we not prophesied in thy name? and in thy name have cast out devils? and in thy name done many</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:534.67px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">wonderful works?  7:23 And then will I profess unto them, I never knew you: depart from me, ye that</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:548.71px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">work iniquity. 7:24 Therefore whosoever heareth these sayings of mine, and doeth them, I will liken</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:562.75px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">him unto a wise man, which built his house upon a rock: 7:25 And the rain descended, and the floods</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:576.79px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">came, and the winds blew, and beat upon that house; and it fell not: for it was founded upon a rock.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:590.83px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">7:26 And every one that heareth these sayings of mine, and doeth them not, shall be likened unto a</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:604.78px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">foolish man, which built his house upon the sand: 7:27 And the rain descended, and the floods came,</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:618.82px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">and the winds blew, and beat upon that house; and it fell: and great was the fall of it. 7:28 And it came</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:632.86px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">to pass, when Jesus had ended these sayings, the people were astonished at his doctrine: 7:29 For he</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:646.90px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">taught them as one having authority, and not as the scribes.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:293.93px;top:667.06px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">~~~~~~~</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:310.13px;top:699.70px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">81</span></div>
</div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:50%;margin-left:-306px;top:64962px;width:612px;height:792px;border-style:outset;overflow:hidden">
<div style="position:absolute;left:0px;top:0px">
<img src="5fb2c2c4-5f39-11ea-8b25-0cc47a792c0a_id_5fb2c2c4-5f39-11ea-8b25-0cc47a792c0a_files/background082.jpg" width=612 height=792></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:250.13px;top:67.20px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Eating with Publicans (Mk)</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:72.02px;top:83.30px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Publicans, or tax collectors, were unclean for a number of reasons, among which was their handling of</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:97.22px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">pagan currencies and acceptance of bribes. Jesus made a point of associating with such social untouchables</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:111.26px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">and praising their attitude of abject humility before God as opposed to the pride of the sanctimonious.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:125.30px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Pharisees made a point of following the Law to a ludicrous degree, while the Essenes tried to purify</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:139.34px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">themselves, expecting thereby to be admitted to the Kingdom.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:72.02px;top:462.67px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Mt 9:10 And it came to pass, as Jesus sat at meat in the house, behold, many publicans and sinners came</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:476.71px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">and sat down with him and his disciples. 9:11 And when the Pharisees saw it, they said unto his disciples,</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:490.75px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Why eateth your Master with publicans and sinners?  9:12 But when Jesus heard that, he said unto them,</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:504.67px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">They that be whole need not a physician, but they that are sick. 9:13 But go ye and learn what that</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:518.71px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">meaneth, I will have mercy, and not sacrifice: for I am not come to call the righteous, but sinners to</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:532.75px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">repentance.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:293.93px;top:552.91px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">~~~~~~~</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:309.41px;top:699.70px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">82</span></div>
</div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:50%;margin-left:-306px;top:65764px;width:612px;height:792px;border-style:outset;overflow:hidden">
<div style="position:absolute;left:0px;top:0px">
<img src="5fb2c2c4-5f39-11ea-8b25-0cc47a792c0a_id_5fb2c2c4-5f39-11ea-8b25-0cc47a792c0a_files/background083.jpg" width=612 height=792></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:261.65px;top:67.20px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Jesus on Family Values</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:72.02px;top:83.30px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">One must sever family loyalties as the price of discipleship. The traditional Messianic role is rejected.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:99.26px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Mt 10:32 Whosoever therefore shall confess me before men, him will I confess also before my</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:90.02px;top:113.30px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Father which is in heaven. 10:33 But whosoever shall deny me before men, him will I also deny</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:90.02px;top:127.34px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">before my Father which is in heaven. 10:34 Think not that I am come to send peace on earth: I</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:90.02px;top:141.38px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">came not to send peace, but a sword. 10:35 For I am come to set a man at variance against his father,</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:90.02px;top:155.42px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">and the daughter against her mother, and the daughter in law against her mother in law.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:158.18px;top:171.38px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">10:36 And a man's foes shall be they of his own household. Mic 7:6</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:90.02px;top:187.46px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">10:37 He that loveth father or mother more than me is not worthy of me: and he that loveth son</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:90.02px;top:201.50px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">or daughter more than me is not worthy of me. 10:38 And he that taketh not his cross, and</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:90.02px;top:215.54px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">followeth after me, is not worthy of me. 10:39 He that findeth his life shall lose it: and he that</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:90.02px;top:229.58px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">loseth his life for my sake shall find it. 10:40 He that receiveth you receiveth me, and he that</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:90.02px;top:243.50px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">receiveth me receiveth him that sent me. 10:41 He that receiveth a prophet in the name of a</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:90.02px;top:257.57px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">prophet shall receive a prophet's reward; and he that receiveth a righteous man in the name of a</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:90.02px;top:271.61px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">righteous man shall receive a righteous man's reward. 10:42 And whosoever shall give to drink</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:90.02px;top:285.65px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">unto one of these little ones a cup of cold water only in the name of a disciple, verily I say unto you,</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:90.02px;top:299.69px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">he shall in no wise lose his reward. 11:1 And it came to pass, when Jesus had made an end of</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:90.02px;top:313.73px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">commanding his twelve disciples, he departed thence to teach and to preach in their cities.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:306.29px;top:466.75px" class="cls_019"><span class="cls_019">….</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:90.02px;top:481.15px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">12:46 While he yet talked to the people, behold, his mother and his brethren stood without, desiring</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:90.02px;top:495.19px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">to speak with him. 12:47 Then one said unto him, Behold, thy mother and thy brethren stand</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:90.02px;top:509.23px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">without, desiring to speak with thee. 12:48 But he answered and said unto him that told him, Who is</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:90.02px;top:523.27px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">my mother?  and who are my brethren?  12:49 And he stretched forth his hand toward his disciples,</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:90.02px;top:537.31px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">and said, Behold my mother and my brethren! 2:50 For whosoever shall do the will of my Father</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:90.02px;top:551.35px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">which is in heaven, the same is my brother, and sister, and mother.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:293.93px;top:571.39px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">~~~~~~~</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:310.01px;top:699.70px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">83</span></div>
</div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:50%;margin-left:-306px;top:66566px;width:612px;height:792px;border-style:outset;overflow:hidden">
<div style="position:absolute;left:0px;top:0px">
<img src="5fb2c2c4-5f39-11ea-8b25-0cc47a792c0a_id_5fb2c2c4-5f39-11ea-8b25-0cc47a792c0a_files/background084.jpg" width=612 height=792></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:242.93px;top:67.20px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Parable of the Sheep and Goats</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:72.02px;top:83.30px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Jesus here gives a clear protocol for salvation; namely, to help those in need, even anonymously. This is in</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:97.22px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">stark contrast to the criteria for salvation as given by Paul, which became the orthodox teaching; namely,</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:111.26px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">faith in Jesus and baptism. Paul’s logic is that if doing good were enough to warrant entrance into the</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:125.30px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Kingdom of Heaven, then Jesus need not have died upon the cross, which is true: he didn’t need to die</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:139.34px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">that way. Paul, however, was obsessed with the resurrection as the key aspect of Christianity. Thus</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:153.38px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Paul, on his own authority, subverts possibly the single most important teaching of Jesus.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:318.65px;top:169.46px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Mt 25:31 “When the Son of man shall come in his</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:328.01px;top:183.38px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">glory, and all the holy angels with him, then shall</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:328.01px;top:197.42px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">he sit upon the throne of his glory: 25:32 And</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:328.01px;top:211.46px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">before him shall be gathered all nations: and he</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:328.01px;top:225.50px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">shall  separate  them  one  from  another,  as  a</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:328.01px;top:239.54px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">shepherd divideth his sheep from the goats: 25:33</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:328.01px;top:253.61px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">And he shall set the sheep on his right hand, but</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:328.01px;top:267.65px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">the goats on the left. 25:34 Then shall the King</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:328.01px;top:281.69px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">say unto them on his right hand, Come, ye</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:328.01px;top:295.73px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">blessed  of  my  Father,  inherit  the  kingdom</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:328.01px;top:309.77px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">prepared for you from the foundation of the</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:328.01px;top:323.69px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">world: 25:35 For I was an hungred, and ye gave</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:328.01px;top:337.73px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">me meat: I was thirsty, and ye gave me drink: I</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:328.01px;top:351.77px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">was a stranger, and ye took me in: 25:36 Naked,</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:328.01px;top:365.81px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">and ye clothed me: I was sick, and ye visited me:</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:99.02px;top:381.89px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">I was in prison, and ye came unto me. 25:37 Then shall the righteous answer him, saying, Lord,</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:99.02px;top:395.93px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">when saw we thee an hungred, and fed thee? or thirsty, and gave thee drink?  25:38 When saw we</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:99.02px;top:409.85px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">thee a stranger, and took thee in? or naked, and clothed thee?  25:39 Or when saw we thee sick, or in</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:99.02px;top:423.91px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">prison, and came unto thee?  25:40 And the King shall answer and say unto them, Verily I say unto</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:99.02px;top:437.95px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">you, Inasmuch as ye have done it unto one of the least of these my brethren, ye have done it unto me.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:99.02px;top:451.99px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">25:41 Then shall he say also unto them on the left hand, Depart from me, ye cursed, into</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:99.02px;top:466.03px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">everlasting fire, prepared for the devil and his angels: 25:42 For I was an hungred, and ye gave me</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:99.02px;top:480.07px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">no meat: I was thirsty, and ye gave me no drink: 25:43 I was a stranger, and ye took me not in:</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:99.02px;top:494.11px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">naked, and ye clothed me not: sick, and in prison, and ye visited me not. 25:44 Then shall they also</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:99.02px;top:508.15px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">answer him, saying, Lord, when saw we thee an hungred, or athirst, or a stranger, or naked, or sick,</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:99.02px;top:522.19px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">or in prison, and did not minister unto thee?  25:45 Then shall he answer them, saying, Verily I say</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:99.02px;top:536.23px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">unto you, Inasmuch as ye did it not to one of the least of these, ye did it not to me. 25:46 And these</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:99.02px;top:550.15px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">shall go away into everlasting punishment: but the righteous into life eternal.”</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:72.02px;top:566.23px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Jesus’ brother James, leader of the early Church, also emphasized the primacy of charity (good works),</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:72.02px;top:580.27px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">but at his death, church fathers chose Paul’s sacramental model based upon baptism and faith, because if</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:72.02px;top:594.34px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">random kindness is the key to salvation, one really doesn’t need a church.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:293.93px;top:614.38px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">~~~~~~~</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:308.45px;top:699.70px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">84</span></div>
</div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:50%;margin-left:-306px;top:67368px;width:612px;height:792px;border-style:outset;overflow:hidden">
<div style="position:absolute;left:0px;top:0px">
<img src="5fb2c2c4-5f39-11ea-8b25-0cc47a792c0a_id_5fb2c2c4-5f39-11ea-8b25-0cc47a792c0a_files/background085.jpg" width=612 height=792></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:260.93px;top:67.20px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">The Last Supper (Mk)</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:72.02px;top:83.30px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">By dipping his hand into the relish “with” Jesus and not waiting until Jesus as leader had dipped, Judas</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:97.22px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">asserted his leadership over the group, according to one interpretation.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:241.13px;top:284.09px" class="cls_008"><span class="cls_008">The Last Supper Leonardo da Vinci</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:72.02px;top:297.41px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">26:17 Now the first day of the feast of unleavened bread the disciples came to Jesus, saying unto him,</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:311.45px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Where wilt thou that we prepare for thee to eat the passover?  26:18 And he said, Go into the city to</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:325.49px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">such a man, and say unto him, The Master saith, My time is at hand; I will keep the passover at thy</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:339.53px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">house with my disciples. 26:19 And the disciples did as Jesus had appointed them; and they made ready</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:353.57px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">the passover. 26:20 Now when the even was come, he sat down with the twelve. 26:21 And as they did</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:367.49px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">eat, he said, Verily I say unto you, that one of you shall betray me. 26:22 And they were exceeding</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:381.53px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">sorrowful, and began every one of them to say unto him, Lord, is it I?  26:23 And he answered and said,</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:395.57px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">He that dippeth his hand with me in the dish, the same shall betray me. 26:24 The Son of man goeth as</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:409.61px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">it is written of him: but woe unto that man by whom the Son of man is betrayed! it had been good for</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:423.67px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">that man if he had not been born. 26:25 Then Judas, which betrayed him, answered and said, Master, is</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:437.71px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">it I?  He said unto him, Thou hast said. 26:26 And as they were eating, Jesus took bread, and blessed it,</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:451.75px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">and brake it, and gave it to the disciples, and said, Take, eat; this is my body. 26:27 And he took the cup,</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:465.79px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">and gave thanks, and gave it to them, saying, Drink ye all of it; 26:28 For this is my blood of the new</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:479.83px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">testament, which is shed for many for the remission of sins.  26:29 But I say unto you, I will not drink</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:493.75px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">henceforth of this fruit of the vine, until that day when I drink it new with you in my Father's kingdom.</span></div>

<div style="position:absolute;left:271.61px;top:67.20px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Gethsemane (Mk)</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:72.02px;top:83.30px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">There are numerous citations of Zechariah in these last chapters of Matthew, here about the shepherds</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:97.22px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">and the Mount of Olives.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:72.02px;top:349.25px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">26:30 And when they had sung an hymn, they went out into the mount of Olives. 26:31 Then saith Jesus</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:363.29px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">unto them, All ye shall be offended because of me this night: for it is written,</span></div>

<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:395.33px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">26:32 But after I am risen again, I will go before you into Galilee. 26:33 Peter answered and said unto</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:409.37px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">him, Though all men shall be offended because of thee, yet will I never be offended. 26:34 Jesus said</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:423.43px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">unto him, Verily I say unto thee, That this night, before the cock crow, thou shalt deny me thrice. 26:35</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:437.47px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Peter said unto him, Though I should die with thee, yet will I not deny thee. Likewise also said all the</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:451.51px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">disciples. 26:36 Then cometh Jesus with them unto a place called Gethsemane, and saith unto the</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:465.55px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">disciples, Sit ye here, while I go and pray yonder. 26:37 And he took with him Peter and the two sons</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:479.47px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">of Zebedee, and began to be sorrowful and very heavy. 26:38 Then saith he unto them, My soul is</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:493.51px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">exceeding sorrowful, even unto death: tarry ye here, and watch with me. 26:39 And he went a little</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:507.55px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">farther, and fell on his face, and prayed, saying, O my Father, if it be possible, let this cup pass from me:</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:521.59px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">nevertheless not as I will, but as thou wilt. 26:40 And he cometh unto the disciples, and findeth them</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:535.63px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">asleep, and saith unto Peter, What, could ye not watch with me one hour?  26:41 Watch and pray, that</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:549.67px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">ye enter not into temptation: the spirit indeed is willing, but the flesh is weak. 26:42 He went away</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:563.71px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">again the second time, and prayed, saying, O my Father, if this cup may not pass away from me, except</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:577.75px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">I drink it, thy will be done. 26:43 And he came and found them asleep again: for their eyes were heavy.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:591.82px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">26:44 And he left them, and went away again, and prayed the third time, saying the same words.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:605.86px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">26:45 Then cometh he to his disciples, and saith unto them, Sleep on now, and take your rest: behold,</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:619.78px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">the hour is at hand, and the Son of man is betrayed into the hands of sinners.26:46 Rise, let us be going:</span></div>

<div style="position:absolute;left:284.69px;top:67.20px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Arrest (Mk)</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:72.02px;top:83.30px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">John tells us that Judas left the group during the dinner. In greeting Jesus first, Judas again abrogates the</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:97.22px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">relationship required by protocol. It is noteworthy that at least one of Jesus’ followers was armed - a</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:111.26px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">violation of Roman law and indication that an armed revolution was within their expectations of this</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:125.30px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Messiah. This also explains Judas’ betrayal of Jesus in that Judas hopes by revealing that Jesus considers</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:139.34px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">himself the King of the Jews to force Jesus to take miraculous action.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:268.61px;top:366.53px" class="cls_008"><span class="cls_008">Kiss of Judas by Giotto</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:72.02px;top:379.85px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Mt 26:47 And while he yet spake, lo, Judas, one of the twelve, came, and with him a great multitude with</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:393.89px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">swords and staves, from the chief priests and elders of the people. 26:48 Now he that betrayed him</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:407.93px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">gave them a sign, saying, Whomsoever I shall kiss, that same is he: hold him fast. 26:49 And forthwith</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:421.99px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">he came to Jesus, and said, Hail, master; and kissed him. 26:50 And Jesus said unto him, Friend,</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:436.03px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">wherefore art thou come? Then came they, and laid hands on Jesus and took him. 26:51 And, behold,</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:450.07px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">one of them which were with Jesus stretched out his hand, and drew his sword, and struck a servant of</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:464.11px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">the high priest's, and smote off his ear. 26:52 Then said Jesus unto him, Put up again thy sword into his</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:478.03px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">place: for all they that take the sword shall perish with the sword. 26:53 Thinkest thou that I cannot now</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:492.07px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">pray to my Father, and he shall presently give me more than twelve legions of angels?  26:54 But how</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:506.11px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">then shall the scriptures be fulfilled, that thus it must be?</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:362.72px;top:506.11px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">26:55 In that same hour said Jesus to the</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:520.15px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">multitudes, Are ye come out as against a thief with swords and staves for to take me? I sat daily with</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:534.19px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">you teaching in the temple, and ye laid no hold on me. 26:56 But all this was done, that the scriptures of</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:548.23px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">the prophets might be fulfilled. Then all the disciples forsook him, and fled.</span></div>

<div style="position:absolute;left:256.49px;top:67.20px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Before the Council (Mk)</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:72.02px;top:83.30px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Claiming to be the Messiah was not technically blasphemous, but was traitorous to Rome. Messiahship</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:97.22px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">including leading an armed revolt. The evangelist seems clearly to be attempting to shift blame for the</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:111.26px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">crucifixion from the Romans to the Jews.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:259.49px;top:343.73px" class="cls_008"><span class="cls_008">Jesus before the High Priest</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:72.02px;top:357.05px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">26:57 And they that had laid hold on Jesus led him away to Caiaphas the high priest, where the scribes and</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:371.09px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">the elders were assembled. 26:58 But Peter followed him afar off unto the high priest's palace, and</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:385.01px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">went in, and sat with the servants, to see the end. 26:59 Now the chief priests, and elders, and all the</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:399.05px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">council, sought false witness against Jesus, to put him to death; 26:60 But found none: yea, though</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:413.09px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">many false witnesses came, yet found they none. At the last came two false witnesses, 26:61 And said,</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:427.15px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">This fellow said, I am able to destroy the temple of God, and to build it in three days. 26:62 And the</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:441.19px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">high priest arose, and said unto him, Answerest thou nothing? what is it which these witness against</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:455.23px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">thee?  26:63 But Jesus held his peace, And the high priest answered and said unto him, I adjure thee by</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:469.27px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">the living God, that thou tell us whether thou be the Christ, the Son of God. 26:64 Jesus saith unto him,</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:483.31px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Thou hast said: nevertheless I say unto you,</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:116.18px;top:499.27px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Hereafter shall ye see the Son of man sitting on the right hand of power, and coming in</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:232.97px;top:513.31px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">the clouds of heaven. Daniel 7:13 ff.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:529.39px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">26:65 Then the high priest rent his clothes, saying, He hath spoken blasphemy; what further need have</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:543.43px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">we of witnesses? behold, now ye have heard his blasphemy. 26:66 What think ye? They answered and</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:557.35px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">said, He is guilty of death. 26:67 Then did they spit in his face, and buffeted him; and others smote</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:571.39px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">him with the palms of their hands, 26:68 Saying, Prophesy unto us, thou Christ, Who is he that smote</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:585.43px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">thee?</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:293.93px;top:605.62px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">~~~~~~~</span></div>

<div style="position:absolute;left:268.85px;top:67.20px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Death of Judas (Q)</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:72.02px;top:83.30px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Mistranslation of Zecherian prophecy, misattribution to Jeremiah. Also, Matthew’s account differs from</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:97.22px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">that in Acts1:18 “Now this man purchased a field with the wages of iniquity; and falling headlong he</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:111.26px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">burst open in the middle and all his entrails gushed out.” Some artistic portrayals incorporate both</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:125.30px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">legends.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:72.02px;top:141.38px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Mt 27:3 Then Judas, which had betrayed him, when</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:155.42px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">he saw that he was condemned, repented himself,</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:169.46px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">and brought again the thirty pieces of silver to the</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:183.38px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">chief priests and elders,</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:209.59px;top:183.38px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">27:4 Saying, I have</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:197.42px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">sinned in that I have betrayed the innocent blood.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:211.46px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">And they said, What is that to us? see thou to</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:225.50px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">that. 27:5 And he cast down the pieces of silver in</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:239.54px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">the temple, and departed, and went and hanged</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:253.61px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">himself. 27:6 And the chief priests took the silver</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:267.65px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">pieces, and said, It is not lawful for to put them</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:281.69px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">into the treasury, because it is the price of blood.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:295.73px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">27:7 And they took counsel, and bought with</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:309.77px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">them the potter's field, to bury strangers in. 27:8</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:323.69px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Wherefore that field was called, The field of</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:337.73px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">blood, unto this day. 27:9 Then was fulfilled that</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:351.77px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">which was spoken by Jeremy the prophet, saying,</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:99.02px;top:367.85px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">And they took the thirty pieces of silver,</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:100.70px;top:381.89px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">the price of him that was valued, whom</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:102.02px;top:395.93px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">they of the children of Israel did value;</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:105.38px;top:409.85px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">27:10 And gave them for the potter's</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:116.30px;top:423.91px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">field, as the Lord appointed me.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:164.54px;top:439.99px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Zec 11:12-13</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:293.93px;top:461.95px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">~~~~~~~</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:271.37px;top:475.99px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Questioning (Mk)</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:72.02px;top:492.07px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Pilate goes directly to the point of the arrest. Though we have no record of Jesus calling himself King of</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:506.11px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">the Jews publicly, someone told Pilate that he had - Judas!</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:318.65px;top:537.55px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Mt 27:11 And Jesus stood before the governor: and</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:327.65px;top:551.59px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">the governor asked him, saying, Art thou the</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:327.65px;top:565.63px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">King of the Jews? And Jesus said unto him, Thou</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:327.65px;top:579.67px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">sayest. 27:12 And when he was accused of the</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:327.65px;top:593.74px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">chief priests and elders, he answered nothing.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:327.65px;top:607.66px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">27:13 Then said Pilate unto him, Hearest thou not</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:327.65px;top:621.70px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">how many things they witness against thee?  27:14</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:327.65px;top:635.74px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">And he answered him to never a word; insomuch</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:327.65px;top:649.78px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">that the governor marvelled greatly.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:293.93px;top:683.50px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">~~~~~~~</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:309.17px;top:699.70px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">89</span></div>
</div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:50%;margin-left:-306px;top:71378px;width:612px;height:792px;border-style:outset;overflow:hidden">
<div style="position:absolute;left:0px;top:0px">
<img src="5fb2c2c4-5f39-11ea-8b25-0cc47a792c0a_id_5fb2c2c4-5f39-11ea-8b25-0cc47a792c0a_files/background090.jpg" width=612 height=792></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:279.89px;top:67.20px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Barabbas (Mk)</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:72.02px;top:83.30px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Why in the world would Pilate release an insurrectionist on the eve of Passover? There is no external</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:97.22px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">attestation of such a process. Also, his name seems a bit too generic: Bar-abbas - ‘son of the father.’ This</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:111.26px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">seems to be an attempt to further inculpate the Jews in Jesus’ death.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:72.02px;top:127.34px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">27:15 Now at that feast the governor was wont to</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:141.38px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">release unto the people a prisoner, whom they</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:155.42px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">would.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:121.45px;top:155.42px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">27:16  And  they  had  then  a  notable</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:169.46px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">prisoner, called Barabbas. 27:17 Therefore when</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:183.38px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">they were gathered together, Pilate said unto</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:197.42px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">them, Whom will ye that I release unto you?</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:211.46px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Barabbas, or Jesus which is called Christ?</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:287.26px;top:211.46px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">27:18</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:225.50px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">For he knew that for envy they had delivered him.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:239.54px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">27:19 When he was set down on the judgment</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:253.61px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">seat, his wife sent unto him, saying, Have thou</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:267.65px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">nothing to do with that just man: for I have</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:281.69px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">suffered many things this day in a dream because</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:295.73px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">of him. 27:20 But the chief priests and elders</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:309.77px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">persuaded the multitude that they should ask</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:323.69px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Barabbas, and destroy Jesus. 27:21 The governor</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:337.73px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">answered and said unto them, Whether of the</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:351.77px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">twain will ye that I release unto you? They said,</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:365.81px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Barabbas. 27:22 Pilate saith unto them, What</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:379.85px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">shall I do then with Jesus which is called Christ?</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:393.89px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">They all say unto him, Let him be crucified. 27:23</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:407.93px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">And the governor said, Why, what evil hath he</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:421.99px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">done? But they cried out the more, saying, Let</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:436.03px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">him be crucified. 27:24 When Pilate saw that he</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:449.95px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">could prevail nothing, but that rather a tumult</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:463.99px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">was made, he took water, and washed his hands</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:480.07px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">before the multitude, saying, I am innocent of the blood of this just person: see ye to it. 27:25 Then</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.38px;top:494.11px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">answered all the people,and said, His blood be on us, and on our children. 27:26 Then released he</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.38px;top:508.15px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Barabbas unto them: and when he had scourged Jesus, he delivered him to be crucified.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:298.37px;top:522.19px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">~~~~~~~</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:308.69px;top:699.70px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">90</span></div>
</div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:50%;margin-left:-306px;top:72180px;width:612px;height:792px;border-style:outset;overflow:hidden">
<div style="position:absolute;left:0px;top:0px">
<img src="5fb2c2c4-5f39-11ea-8b25-0cc47a792c0a_id_5fb2c2c4-5f39-11ea-8b25-0cc47a792c0a_files/background091.jpg" width=612 height=792></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:273.17px;top:67.20px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Crucifixion (Mk)</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:72.02px;top:83.30px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">In Luke, one of the bandits repents. The Synoptic Gospels have Simon of Cyrene carrying Jesus’ cross,</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:97.22px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">but John says he bears it himself (John 19:17); furthermore, the Synoptic Gospels have Jesus being</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:111.26px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">crucified on the day after the Passover meal (Last Supper), while John, for poetic effect, has Jesus die</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:125.30px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">as the lambs are being killed for the meal.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:72.02px;top:340.13px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Mt 27:32 And as they came out, they found a man of Cyrene, Simon by name: him they compelled to bear</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:354.17px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">his cross. 27:33 And when they were come unto a place called Golgotha, that is to say, a place of a skull,</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:368.21px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">27:34 They gave him vinegar to drink mingled with gall: and when he had tasted thereof, he would not</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:382.25px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">drink. 27:35 And they crucified him, and parted his garments, casting lots: that it might be fulfilled</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:396.29px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">which was spoken by the prophet, They parted my garments among them, and upon my vesture did</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:410.33px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">they cast lots. 27:36 And sitting down they watched him there; 27:37 And set up over his head his</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:424.39px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">accusation written, THIS IS JESUS THE KING OF THE JEWS. 27:38 Then were there two</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:438.43px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">thieves crucified with him, one on the right hand, and another on the left. 27:39 And they that passed</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:452.35px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">by reviled him, wagging their heads, 27:40 And saying, Thou that destroyest the temple, and buildest</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:466.39px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">it in three days, save thyself. If thou be the Son of God, come down from the cross. 27:41 Likewise also</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:480.43px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">the chief priests mocking him, with the scribes and elders, said, 27:42 He saved others; himself he</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:494.47px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">cannot save. If he be the King of Israel, let him now come down from the cross, and we will believe him.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:508.51px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">27:43 He trusted in God; let him deliver him now, if he will have him: for he said, I am the Son of God.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:522.55px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">27:44 The thieves also, which were crucified with him, cast the same in his teeth.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:293.93px;top:542.59px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">~~~~~~~</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:310.25px;top:699.70px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">91</span></div>
</div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:50%;margin-left:-306px;top:72982px;width:612px;height:792px;border-style:outset;overflow:hidden">
<div style="position:absolute;left:0px;top:0px">
<img src="5fb2c2c4-5f39-11ea-8b25-0cc47a792c0a_id_5fb2c2c4-5f39-11ea-8b25-0cc47a792c0a_files/background092.jpg" width=612 height=792></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:285.65px;top:67.20px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Death (Mk)</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:72.02px;top:83.30px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Darkness from noon to 3:00 pm, reminiscent of the darkness over Egypt before the first Passover, was</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:97.22px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">most probably added for dramatic effect, as were the sheeted dead emerging from their tombs. Based</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:111.26px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">on his “Eli…” citation, Jesus apparently learned the Psalms in Aramaic. Elias (Elijah) was a prophet who</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:125.30px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">did not die, but was taken up into Heaven by a chariot of fire, and would come to the aid of the</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:139.34px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">distressed. Josephus has an account of an earthquake before the fall of Jerusalem in 70. Mt: John; Mk</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:153.38px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">14-15, John 18-19, died on different days. Note also that none of his followers was present, but only</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:167.42px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">some women “beholding afar off.”</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:72.02px;top:439.03px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Mt 27:45 Now from the sixth hour there was darkness over all the land unto the ninth hour. 27:46 And</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:453.07px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">about the ninth hour Jesus cried with a loud voice, saying,</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:238.37px;top:469.15px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Eli, Eli, lama sabachthani? Ps 22:1</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:485.11px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">that is to say, My God, my God, why hast thou forsaken me?  27:47 Some of them that stood there,</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:499.15px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">when they heard that, said, This man calleth for Elias. 27:48 And straightway one of them ran, and</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:513.19px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">took a spunge, and filled it with vinegar, and put it on a reed, and gave him to drink. 27:49 The rest</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:527.23px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">said, Let be, let us see whether Elias will come to save him. 27:50 Jesus, when he had cried again with a</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:541.27px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">loud voice, yielded up the ghost. 27:51 And, behold, the veil of the temple was rent in twain from the</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:555.31px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">top to the bottom; and the earth did quake, and the rocks rent; 27:52 And the graves were opened; and</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:569.35px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">many bodies of the saints which slept arose, 27:53 And came out of the graves after his resurrection, and</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:583.39px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">went into the holy city, and appeared unto many. 27:54 Now when the centurion, and they that were</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:597.46px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">with him, watching Jesus, saw the earthquake, and those things that were done, they feared greatly,</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:611.38px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">saying, Truly this was the Son of God. 27:55 And many women were there beholding afar off, which</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:625.42px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">followed Jesus from Galilee, ministering unto him: 27:56 Among which was Mary Magdalene, and</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:639.46px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Mary the mother of James and Joses, and the mother of Zebedees children.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:293.93px;top:659.62px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">~~~~~~~</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:309.53px;top:699.70px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">92</span></div>
</div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:50%;margin-left:-306px;top:73784px;width:612px;height:792px;border-style:outset;overflow:hidden">
<div style="position:absolute;left:0px;top:0px">
<img src="5fb2c2c4-5f39-11ea-8b25-0cc47a792c0a_id_5fb2c2c4-5f39-11ea-8b25-0cc47a792c0a_files/background093.jpg" width=612 height=792></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:286.61px;top:67.20px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Burial (Mk)</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:72.02px;top:83.30px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Joseph, a member of the very Council that had unanimously condemned Jesus to death, sought Jesus’</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:97.22px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">body secretly from Pilate according to John 19:38. Josephus relates that bodies of crucified criminals</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:111.26px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">were taken down and buried before evening of the Sabbath. Criminals were sometimes secretly</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:125.30px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">rescued in this way. Legs were broken to hasten death.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:72.02px;top:482.35px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Mt 27:57 When the even was come, there came a rich man of Arimathaea, named Joseph, who also</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:496.39px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">himself was Jesus' disciple: 27:58 He went to Pilate, and begged the body of Jesus. Then Pilate</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:510.31px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">commanded the body to be delivered. 27:59 And when Joseph had taken the body, he wrapped it in a</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:524.35px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">clean linen cloth, 27:60 And laid it in his own new tomb, which he had hewn out in the rock: and he</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:538.39px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">rolled a great stone to the door of the sepulchre, and departed. 27:61 And there was Mary Magdalene,</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:552.43px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">and the other Mary, sitting over against the sepulchre. 27:62 Now the next day, that followed the day</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:566.47px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">of the preparation, the chief priests and Pharisees came together unto Pilate, 27:63 Saying, Sir, we</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:580.51px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">remember that that deceiver said, while he was yet alive, After three days I will rise again. 27:64</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:594.58px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Command therefore that the sepulchre be made sure until the third day, lest his disciples come by night,</span></div>
