<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:608.62px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">and steal him away, and say unto the people, He is risen from the dead: so the last error shall be worse</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:622.66px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">than the first. 27:65 Pilate said unto them, Ye have a watch: go your way, make it as sure as ye can.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:636.70px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">27:66 So they went, and made the sepulchre sure, sealing the stone, and setting a watch.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:293.93px;top:656.74px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">~~~~~~~</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:310.01px;top:699.70px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">93</span></div>
</div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:50%;margin-left:-306px;top:74586px;width:612px;height:792px;border-style:outset;overflow:hidden">
<div style="position:absolute;left:0px;top:0px">
<img src="5fb2c2c4-5f39-11ea-8b25-0cc47a792c0a_id_5fb2c2c4-5f39-11ea-8b25-0cc47a792c0a_files/background094.jpg" width=612 height=792></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:269.81px;top:67.20px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Resurrection (Mk)</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:72.02px;top:83.30px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Mark had no tradition of a sealed and guarded tomb, and the women came merely to dress the body,</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:97.22px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">which is far more likely. Luke has the Apostles meeting Jesus in Emmaeus, a suburb of Jerusalem. The</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:111.26px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">difference between Galilee and Jerusalem as the point of meeting may reflect tension between the</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:125.30px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Christians of Galilee (north) and those of Judea (south). ‘Extension’(MkX) refers to the continuation</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:139.34px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">of the Gospel of Mark added during the Middle Ages. The original ends at Mark 16:8.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:72.02px;top:155.42px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Who went to the tomb:</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:72.02px;top:169.46px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Magdalene (Mk, Mt, L, J), Mary mother of James (Mk, Mt, L), Salome (Mk), Joanna (L), Galilean</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:183.50px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">women (L)</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:72.02px;top:201.50px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">What was seen:</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:72.02px;top:215.66px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Stone already rolled away (Mk, L, J), angel rolls back stone (Mt), one man (Mk, Mt), two men (L, J)</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:318.65px;top:233.54px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">What was done:</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:318.65px;top:247.61px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Told he is risen (Mk, Mt, L), they flee (Mk), Jesus</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:318.65px;top:261.65px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">appears to Magdalene, then two others, then to the</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:318.65px;top:275.69px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">eleven, he gives commission, he ascends (Mk X);</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:318.65px;top:289.61px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Magdalene and “the other Mary” meet him, hold</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:318.65px;top:303.65px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">his feet (Mt); the women tell the apostles, who not</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:318.65px;top:317.69px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">believe them, Peter runs, sees linen, Jesus appears</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:318.65px;top:331.73px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">to Cleopas (Simon?), is not recognized, teaches, is</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:318.65px;top:345.77px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">recognized, vanishes, appears to the eleven, eats,</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:318.65px;top:359.81px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">gives commission, ascends (L); Magdalene tells</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:318.65px;top:373.85px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">John and Peter the body has been taken, they run,</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:318.65px;top:387.89px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">see the linen, leave, Magdalene sees Jesus, thinks he</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:318.65px;top:401.93px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">is the gardener, recognizes him, told not to touch</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:318.65px;top:415.85px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">him, Jesus appears to the eleven, breathes the Holy</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:318.65px;top:429.91px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Ghost on them; eight days later Jesus again appears</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:318.65px;top:443.95px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">to Thomas, later appears again, helps them fish (J).</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:72.02px;top:457.99px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Where are the Apostles to meet Jesus?    Galilee (Mk, Mt), Jerusalem (MkX, L, J)</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:290.69px;top:478.03px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">~~~~~~~~</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:258.29px;top:492.07px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Final Commission (Mk)</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:72.02px;top:508.15px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">The baptismal injunction seems to be from a post-Nicene orthodoxy.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:72.02px;top:524.11px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Mt 28:16 Then the eleven disciples went away into Galilee, into a mountain where Jesus had appointed</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:538.15px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">them. 28:17 And when they saw him, they worshipped him: but some doubted. 28:18 And Jesus came</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:552.19px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">and spake unto them, saying,</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:199.58px;top:568.15px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">All power is given unto me in heaven and in earth.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:191.30px;top:584.23px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">28:19 Go ye therefore, and teach all nations, Dan 7:14</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:600.34px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">baptizing them in the name of the Father, and of the Son, and of the Holy Ghost: 28:20 Teaching them</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:614.26px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">to observe all things whatsoever I have commanded you: and, lo, I am with you alway, even unto the</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:628.30px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">end of the world. Amen.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:290.93px;top:644.38px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">~~~~~~~~</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:308.45px;top:699.70px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">94</span></div>
</div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:50%;margin-left:-306px;top:75388px;width:612px;height:792px;border-style:outset;overflow:hidden">
<div style="position:absolute;left:0px;top:0px">
<img src="5fb2c2c4-5f39-11ea-8b25-0cc47a792c0a_id_5fb2c2c4-5f39-11ea-8b25-0cc47a792c0a_files/background095.jpg" width=612 height=792></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:248.57px;top:67.20px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">So then, why believe?</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:72.02px;top:83.30px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">So, given the glaring inconsistencies, anachronisms, evidence of tampering, etc., what then would induce</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:97.22px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">otherwise intelligent people to believe steadfastly, or at least profess to believe, in the infallibility of</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:111.26px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">these doctrines? There are numerous reasons to do so, some nobler than others.  There is a</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:125.30px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">considerable degree of overlap between them.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:72.02px;top:141.38px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Here are the reasons gathered and categorized so far, given alphabetically:</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:72.02px;top:157.34px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Ambition: Armed with a few quotes from the Apostle Paul, a person can speak with authority and climb</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:171.38px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">as high as her temerity will allow. Wrapped in the cloak of righteousness, she can attack all enemies with</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:185.42px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">impunity and then, when attacked in return, hide behind the crucifix. Now she can go out and impose</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:199.46px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">“God’s Word” on the larger sphere. She now has a host of new powers to impose on the world, perhaps</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:213.50px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">to shame and intimidate, perhaps to self-righteously condemn, perhaps to take an authoritative role in a</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:227.54px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">discussion or decision, perhaps to feel superior through comfort or “spiritual” advice; always aiming at a</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:241.58px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">position of control “in the name of God.” We all know well enough to what horrific ends these powers</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:255.65px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">will reach if unchecked: burning “heretics” alive, etc.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:271.61px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">A church, no matter how small, is often the arena for personality struggles between its members, for</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:285.65px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">whom faith is an opportunity to exert dominance. When a religious establishment dominates a town, it</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:299.69px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">becomes the rostrum for social ascension.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:72.02px;top:315.77px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Authority: How dare I doubt when great and learned men and women before have expressed firm belief?</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:329.69px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">What right have I to doubt their authority? What do I know that they didn’t? They can’t all be wrong,</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:343.73px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">can they?</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:359.81px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">When both parents and other authoritative figures in society insist upon the truth of a certain belief,</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:373.85px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">who has the gumption to question it? Lack of intellectual confidence goes a long way to explain this</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:387.89px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">impulse. Then, when children discover inconsistencies in their religion, they are merely told that it’s a</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:401.93px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">“mystery” and they must accept it on “faith.””Blessed are those that have not seen, yet still believe.”</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:72.02px;top:417.89px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Class struggle: Both Christianity and Buddhism prospered initially because they appealed to a large</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:431.95px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">underclass with little hope of social advancement under the pre-Christian/pre-Buddhist social</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:445.99px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">hierarchy. Churches offer them a glimpse of equality and self-importance.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:318.65px;top:461.95px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Comfort in distress through resignation to God’s</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:327.65px;top:475.99px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Will - In The Brothers Karamazov, as the Elder</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:327.65px;top:490.03px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Zosima attempts to comfort the woman whose</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:327.65px;top:504.07px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">children have all died, he goes through the usual</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:327.65px;top:518.11px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">laundry list of pious explanations: your child is in</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:327.65px;top:532.15px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Heaven now looking down on us; God is testing</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:327.65px;top:546.19px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">your faith; etc. The best consolation for the</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:327.65px;top:560.23px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">bereaved is the belief that they are in a better place</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:327.65px;top:574.27px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">and that we’ll see them again if we submit to the</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:327.65px;top:588.31px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">church.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:72.02px;top:604.30px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Community: A powerful carrot and a stick. Members support each other emotionally and economically</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:618.34px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">to keep the community as a whole alive. I know of many people who depend on church associations for</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:632.38px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">their livelihood. If they were to question doctrine, they would endanger the economic viability of their</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:646.42px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">way of life. Is it worth it, just to exercise your “freedom of thought” to call down upon you and your</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:660.46px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">family the rage of the community that feeds you? Religious communities also offer safety in numbers.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:674.50px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">The need to belong is basic in human beings: a need satisfied by the military, sports teams, schools,</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:309.65px;top:699.70px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">95</span></div>
</div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:50%;margin-left:-306px;top:76190px;width:612px;height:792px;border-style:outset;overflow:hidden">
<div style="position:absolute;left:0px;top:0px">
<img src="5fb2c2c4-5f39-11ea-8b25-0cc47a792c0a_id_5fb2c2c4-5f39-11ea-8b25-0cc47a792c0a_files/background096.jpg" width=612 height=792></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:67.20px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">gangs, and churches. This is especially true in smaller “religious” towns, where everyone knows who the</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:81.26px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">doubter is among them. Shunning is thus a potent tool to keep people on the straight and narrow,</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:95.30px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">whether they really believe the doctrine or not. Mob psychology is an effective form of enforcing unity.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:109.34px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">The primal fear of isolation or dying alone is also soothed by church communities. Persecution also</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:123.38px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">tightens community bonds and portrays the doubter as a treasonous coward.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:72.02px;top:139.34px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Confusion: People who feel overwhelmed and disoriented by life can get soothing, authoritative,</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:153.38px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">narcotizing answers to dilemmas such as global warming, overpopulation, nuclear proliferation, death</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:167.42px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">of children, social injustice, and terrorism.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:72.02px;top:183.38px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Diffidence: People who fear being seen as prideful, or who actually have low self-esteem, can find</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:197.42px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">strength within themselves to go beyond their self-imposed limitations, and can ascribe that strength</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:211.46px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">not to their puny egos, but to a “higher power.” In so doing, they can parade their talents, but only so</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:225.50px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">long as all credit is given to this higher power, so as to shield them from seeming proud (which they are).</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:239.54px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">This externalization of praise and blame empowers people to commit acts of greater courage or of</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:253.61px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">greater cruelty than they thought possible, while under the sway of the “spirit.” Ironically, the more</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:267.65px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">intelligent a person is, the less confidence one has in her own judgment. Thus do many geniuses fall prey</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:281.69px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">to theological nonsense.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:72.02px;top:297.65px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Escapism: Sometimes, the reaction to an unsatisfying life is to escape to the imaginary, narcotizing True</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:311.69px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">World of religion - the apocalypse, the afterlife - or back to a glorious past (that never existed)</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:325.73px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">associated with "old time religion" (meaning Catholicism?) Encouraged by “faith,” one can deny the</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:339.77px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">realities of an inconvenient world, expunge guilt, and overcome shame.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:320.81px;top:355.85px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Family harmony: “Our mother would turn over in</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:327.65px;top:369.77px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">her grave, if she knew that you had left the</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:327.65px;top:383.81px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">church!” Deviating from the family’s religion</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:327.65px;top:397.85px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">entails friction and risk. Finally breaking with the</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:327.65px;top:411.89px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">superstitions supported by a family for</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:327.65px;top:425.95px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">generations requires great courage and</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:327.65px;top:439.99px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">confidence. Yet even then, the knowledge that</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:327.65px;top:454.03px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">certain family members - especially the older or</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:327.65px;top:468.07px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">less sophisticated folks respected and beloved</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:327.65px;top:482.11px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">from childhood - will feel heart-broken or</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:327.65px;top:496.15px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">betrayed is a significant incentive to postpone or</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:327.65px;top:510.07px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">cancel one’s “selfish, prideful” free-thinking.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:72.02px;top:526.15px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Fear: There are manifold fears associated with religion: fear of isolation from friends and family, fear of</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:540.19px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">revenge of the “faithful,” fear of Hell (there isn’t really one, right?), fear of the pointlessness of life if</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:554.23px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">you are right that we are just random emanations of energy hurtling through space, fear of dying alone.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:568.27px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Religion overcomes fear by embracing it (bolstered by the guarantee of an afterlife not merely of</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:582.31px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">physical security, but of permanent ecstasy). Religion harnesses and makes sense out of primal fears: the</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:596.26px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Absurd here corresponds to Nietzsche’s Dionysian impulse; the Individual Unconscious acts as an</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:610.30px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">eddy in the Collective, individuated by trauma: hence the irresistible allure of Hitler, ISIS, Trump,</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:624.34px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">religion. To this category belong superstitions of various forms: seeking security in a frightening world,</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:638.38px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">fear of an afterlife, Then there’s the Existential fear that life is pointless, in answer to which</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:652.42px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">theologians have devised True World theories and championed the Ascetic Ideal. In these thought-</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:666.46px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">experiments, the True World (Heaven) is what matters - this world is a nuisance; the purpose of life</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:680.50px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">is to gain entry into Heaven. This solution solves the need for purpose in life and panders to people’s</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:308.69px;top:699.70px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">96</span></div>
</div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:50%;margin-left:-306px;top:76992px;width:612px;height:792px;border-style:outset;overflow:hidden">
<div style="position:absolute;left:0px;top:0px">
<img src="5fb2c2c4-5f39-11ea-8b25-0cc47a792c0a_id_5fb2c2c4-5f39-11ea-8b25-0cc47a792c0a_files/background097.jpg" width=612 height=792></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:67.20px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">need for self-esteem, while making their salvation the central concern of all creation (It really is all about</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:81.26px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">me!).</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:72.02px;top:97.22px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Feminism: The Cult of Domesticity conceded to women the field of spirituality, and from the earliest</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:111.26px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">days of the church, women played important roles that allowed them a channel to vent their frustrations</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:125.30px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">with paternalistic society. Church is sometimes the only venue for women to express themselves,</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:139.34px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">pseudo-St. Paul notwithstanding.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:318.65px;top:155.42px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Financial Enrichment: A decent living can be made</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:327.65px;top:169.46px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">by offering a range of religious services. I still</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:327.65px;top:183.38px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">recall Reverend Ike on the radio as I drove across</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:327.65px;top:197.42px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">South Carolina in the 1970’s. “For a double</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:327.65px;top:211.46px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">portion gift, you get a double portion blessing!”</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:327.65px;top:225.50px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Evangelism is the last refuge for those who</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:327.65px;top:239.54px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">couldn’t make a living selling shoes.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:318.65px;top:255.65px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Game Theory: Believing entails less risk than not</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:327.65px;top:269.69px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">believing because if there are a Heaven and Hell,</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:327.65px;top:283.61px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">I’m better off covering my bets by believing,</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:327.65px;top:297.65px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">while if there are no such places, I lose nothing.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:318.65px;top:313.73px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Goodness booster shot: Some persons go to church</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:327.65px;top:327.77px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">for the inspiration to be a better person, and it</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:327.65px;top:341.81px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">seems to work: church-goers generally tend to try</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:327.65px;top:355.85px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">to be nicer people.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:72.02px;top:371.81px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Guilt: One of the most despicable psychological methods used to coerce people into church is to project</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:385.85px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">upon them, from earliest youth, guilt for actions that supposedly happened long ago. The first thing</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:399.89px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">these “loving parents” do is to burden the minds of their trusting children with the idea that they are</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:413.93px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">sinful, utterly depraved, and deserve damnation, and God knows every thought you have! The</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:427.99px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Catholic Church is especially skilled at this one, having a sacrament whereby all you need to do is tell the</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:442.03px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">priest every sinful action or unclean thought you have ever had, then you’re magically forgiven and the</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:455.95px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">sins disappear from your soul! Another angle on guilt is the progression:</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:110.18px;top:472.03px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">“The church educated you; your good religious parents raised you; the church community</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:108.02px;top:486.07px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">supported you to go to that damned college where you learned to betray the trust of everyone</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:108.02px;top:500.11px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">who should matter in your life. You’re just on an ego trip! You arrogant ass, how you love to</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:108.02px;top:514.15px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">sneer at the beliefs of good, kind people that crave comfort in their hour of need! What do you</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:108.02px;top:528.19px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">have to offer in the place of our ‘superstition’? Science?!”</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:72.02px;top:544.15px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Hope: In times of desperation and loneliness, people need hope. Militant Islam has arisen at this time</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:558.19px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">because the once-proud kingdoms of the Middle East have been effectively castrated for the last two</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:572.23px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">hundred years. Religion becomes an integral part of individual identity. Submission (like a frontal</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:586.27px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">lobotomy) is the path to happiness. Righteousness becomes the armor and weaponry of social outcasts.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:600.34px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Those whose lives suck, who have been disappointed in love or career, can find acceptance, consolation,</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:614.38px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">and power. This is an especially effective lure to those without hope of improvement of their lot - the</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:628.42px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">chronically poor, the outcasts, druggies, the defeated. The promise of a better life in the next world to</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:642.34px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">those who bear their fate in obedience to God (the church) is balm to their hurt minds. Conversely,</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:656.38px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">former addicts often cite religion as the key to their rehabilitation. Half-way houses run by churches</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:670.42px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">often actually help people get back on their feet.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:309.17px;top:699.70px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">97</span></div>
</div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:50%;margin-left:-306px;top:77794px;width:612px;height:792px;border-style:outset;overflow:hidden">
<div style="position:absolute;left:0px;top:0px">
<img src="5fb2c2c4-5f39-11ea-8b25-0cc47a792c0a_id_5fb2c2c4-5f39-11ea-8b25-0cc47a792c0a_files/background098.jpg" width=612 height=792></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:72.02px;top:67.20px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Immortality: The idea of death is abhorrent to many, so they gravitate to a belief system that satisfies</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:81.26px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">their egotism.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:318.65px;top:97.22px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Indoctrination: “Why do you believe that?”</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:327.65px;top:111.26px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">“Because the church says so. There is nothing you</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:327.65px;top:125.30px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">or anyone can say that will ever shake my faith!”</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:327.65px;top:139.34px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">“Ok, but faith in what?” “I believe whatever the</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:327.65px;top:153.38px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">church says I should believe!” The church is the</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:327.65px;top:167.42px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">font of religious Truth, and like the Communist</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:327.65px;top:181.46px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Party, cannot err. Pope Pius IX said so!</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:327.65px;top:197.42px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">From earliest childhood children are</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:327.65px;top:211.46px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">indoctrinated to accept absurdities as truths, and</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:327.65px;top:225.50px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">any wavering or questioning is treated as heresy.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:318.65px;top:241.58px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Inertia: Many of the less thoughtful among us</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:327.65px;top:255.65px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">believe out of mere laziness.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:318.65px;top:271.61px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Intellectual curiosity: People cannot accept that we</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:327.65px;top:285.65px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">are nothing more than random emanations of</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:327.65px;top:299.69px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">cosmic energy. Their egos demand that we are</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:327.65px;top:313.73px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">more central to the plan, that we are the purpose</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:327.65px;top:327.77px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">of the entirety of creation.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:72.02px;top:343.85px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Intellectual insecurity: People who were never very intelligent find an easy way to take the moral high</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:357.89px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">ground and stand up to the smarty-pants secular humanists. Likewise, persons cognizant of their own</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:371.93px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">intellectual limitations are easily convinced to swallow church doctrine hook, line, and sinker.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:72.02px;top:387.89px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Justice: Those who can't let injustice have the last laugh, who refuse to accept that bad things happen to</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:401.93px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">good people, and that bad people aren’t punished for what they have done, must believe that there is</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:415.97px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">someone keeping score who will dispense justice to the good and evil.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:72.02px;top:431.95px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Justification : Religion is a potent weapon to justify almost any crime against humanity. Slavery was</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:445.99px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">justified by religious leaders quoting the bible, as are wars, both defensive and offensive, opportunistic</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:460.03px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">attacks upon one’s social or economic rivals, and the burning of people at the stake, pogroms, and</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:474.07px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">lynchings - all performed by church-going Christians.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:72.02px;top:490.15px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Loneliness, especially the desire for reunion with loved ones who have died. A local Jehovah’s Witness</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:504.19px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">used to come by from time to time to try to convert me. When I let slip that my mother had died when</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:518.11px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">I was four years old, she immediately went to work on that. The next time she showed up, she had a</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:532.15px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">brochure that showed how I would be reunited with my mother in Heaven, if I joined her group. Here</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:546.19px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">the religious organization plays the dangerous role of quack psychiatrist to people who have suffered</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:560.23px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">emotional trauma, and always with the same prescription: “Complete unquestioning faith in our</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:574.27px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">organization will solve all your problems. Just have faith in (what we tell you about) Jesus.” Conversely,</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:588.31px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">churches also offer a place a stranger can go and have immediate acceptance, a place where she can feel</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:602.38px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">she belongs. The fellowship churches offer also relieves the fear that one will die alone and forgotten.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:616.42px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Seeing friendly, supportive faces once a week is very comforting.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:72.02px;top:632.38px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Masochism: Children who are tricked by their loving parents into believing that the dark shadow of</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:646.42px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">original sin hangs over them, and that the body is inherently “sinful,” not to mention that God knows</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:660.46px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">their every thought (worse than 1984), must be burdened with abundant guilt. Add to that the hidden</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:674.50px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">terror of someone who has actually done something wrong, or whom the doctrine classifies as sexually</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:309.17px;top:699.70px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">98</span></div>
</div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:50%;margin-left:-306px;top:78596px;width:612px;height:792px;border-style:outset;overflow:hidden">
<div style="position:absolute;left:0px;top:0px">
<img src="5fb2c2c4-5f39-11ea-8b25-0cc47a792c0a_id_5fb2c2c4-5f39-11ea-8b25-0cc47a792c0a_files/background099.jpg" width=612 height=792></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:67.20px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">deviant, and it is understandable that many look to religion for a purifying punishment which they</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:81.26px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">know they deserve; hence they welcome punishment and practice asceticism, self-flagellation, etc.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:72.02px;top:97.22px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Morality: Many believe that morals are the proper province of religion rather than philosophy, and that</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:111.26px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Judeo-Christian morals are superior. Morality is taught in churches, so people associate the church with</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:125.30px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">morality, and morality with social order; thus have churches co-opted social mores and claimed a</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:139.34px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">monopoly on goodness, yet too often fail to speak out against the immorality of the flock - hence the</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:153.38px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">acquiescence to slavery from 1619 on, the emergence of the “Southern” (no blacks allowed) Methodist</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:167.42px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">church in 1844, the anti-working class “Acres of Diamonds” gospel of the 1880’s, and the hateful,</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:181.46px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">xenophobic movements against Jews, Catholics, the Irish, Germans, Chinese, gays, and Muslims.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:72.02px;top:197.42px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Mystical Union: People who want to experience the eternal, unchanging seminal power of the universe</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:211.46px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">beyond the reach of reason use various means - meditation, incantations, prayer, a life of selfless service,</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:225.50px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">etc. Churches sometimes offer such paths, but seldom without a load of superstitious nonsense.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:318.65px;top:241.58px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Need for explanations: Personal experience of the</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:327.65px;top:255.65px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">“supernatural” (dreams, lightning on a sunny day,</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:327.65px;top:269.69px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">etc.) requires some explanation, and science</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:327.65px;top:283.61px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">cannot answer every question, yet. Hence, every</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:327.65px;top:297.65px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">unexplained phenomenon becomes a “proof” of</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:327.65px;top:311.69px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">the existence of some deity.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:318.65px;top:327.77px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Nostalgia: Religion manipulates images of</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:327.65px;top:341.81px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">happiness, victory, justice, and order, as well as</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:327.65px;top:355.85px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">the hope of meeting long lost family members or</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:327.65px;top:369.77px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">friends in the next life.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:72.02px;top:385.85px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Philanthropy: For some folks, the doctrine is not as important as the opportunity to serve the needy. In</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:399.89px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">answer to Jesus’ call to clothe the naked, and feed the hungry, like Chaucer’s “pauvre Persoun,” they</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:413.93px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">flock to churches, synagogues, mosques, and temples to help out those in need.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:72.02px;top:429.91px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Philosophical exchange: Some folks like to exchange inspirational ideas with others of generally the same</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:443.95px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">mind, thereby achieving an intellectual high.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:72.02px;top:460.03px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Physical needs: From the beginning, people have turned to gods for basic security. “Give us food, rain,</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:474.07px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">sun, etc.” “Let my child survive this plague.” “Protect our house from this tornado.” “Let our nation</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:488.11px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">repel the invader.” When the seagulls arrive or a child recovers, or the tornado passes them by, or the</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:502.15px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">invader is defeated, it is proof of the efficacy of worship/prayer. What’s interesting are the mental</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:516.07px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">gymnastics exhibited when such help is not forthcoming. The most successful religions have been</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:530.11px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">through cycles of depression and defeat, and have a number of ready rationalizations for failure of</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:544.15px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">divine salvation. Classified under the title of Theodicy, these justifications include such time-worn</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:558.19px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">excuses for the failure of God to protect “his people” as: “We have sinned and are being punished”</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:572.23px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">(often with side-long glances at the presumed guilty party), or “We are being tested,” or “God works</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:586.27px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">in ways beyond our comprehension.” And when an innocent baby dies - “She was guilty of original sin,”</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:600.34px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">or “You’ll see her again in Heaven,” or, strangest of all, “God punishes those whom he loves.”  Supplied</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:614.38px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">with these defense mechanisms, a religion may deflect blame for failing its most basic task and may</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:628.42px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">survive, though diminished, although no one yet can explain where God was during the Holocaust.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:642.34px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">And when even that doesn't account for God’s failures, then cynics turn to apocalypticism, “We live in</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:656.38px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">an evil age, but fear not, the end is near at hand!”</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:309.17px;top:699.70px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">99</span></div>
</div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:50%;margin-left:-306px;top:79398px;width:612px;height:792px;border-style:outset;overflow:hidden">
<div style="position:absolute;left:0px;top:0px">
<img src="5fb2c2c4-5f39-11ea-8b25-0cc47a792c0a_id_5fb2c2c4-5f39-11ea-8b25-0cc47a792c0a_files/background100.jpg" width=612 height=792></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:72.02px;top:67.20px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Political Action: Not only was the abolition movement born out of Great Awakening evangelism, but</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:81.26px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">the temperance and civil rights movements as well. Liberation Theology of the 1960’s mobilized many</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:95.30px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">religious people to take direct political action.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:72.02px;top:111.26px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Political organization: The church is often a positive political agent in a community, as were the black</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:125.30px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">churches during the civil rights movement.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:72.02px;top:141.38px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Pragmatism: Sometimes people join a religion in order to associate with the strongest social class or</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:155.42px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">dominant element; likewise, for an oppressed group, religion is the focus of their strength and security</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:169.46px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">in numbers; further, folks can get a job or find a spouse by joining a certain religious group. Sometimes</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:183.38px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">the motive is to make friends or find a “safe” date.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:72.02px;top:199.46px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Pride: People are unwilling to admit their error, especially after indoctrinating their own children.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:213.50px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Hypocrisy, especially when widely shared, is easier than humiliation.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:72.02px;top:229.58px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Reason for living: People are unwilling to believe that beyond self-gratification their lives are pointless.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:243.50px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Faith is often contrasted to nihilism, wherein life serves no purpose.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:318.65px;top:259.61px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Reason: a) I (or someone whose judgment I trust)</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:327.65px;top:273.65px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">witnessed a miracle (i.e., saw something I/she</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:327.65px;top:287.69px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">can’t explain), so there must be supernatural</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:327.65px;top:301.73px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">phenomena; therefore I will submit to the</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:327.65px;top:315.77px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">doctrine of the church!? b) There must be an</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:327.65px;top:329.69px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">after-life because I have seen dead people in my</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:327.65px;top:343.73px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">dreams. c) This universe cannot have been</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:327.65px;top:357.77px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">random. Humans are too subtle to have evolved</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:327.65px;top:371.81px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">from pond scum. It makes sense to have a</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:327.65px;top:385.85px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">creator-god. d) Scripture is so convincing in its</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:327.65px;top:399.89px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">detail and weighty thought (though that would</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:327.65px;top:413.93px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">also recommend the Mahabharata).</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:318.65px;top:429.91px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Ritual: The grand theater of High Mass with its</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:327.65px;top:443.95px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">majestic sights, sounds, and scents is intoxicating.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:72.02px;top:459.91px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Sadism: Where there is so much desire for correction (see Masochism above), can they be far behind</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:473.83px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">who will gladly dispense the punishment ascribed by Heaven? The Bible unfortunately lends itself</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:487.87px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">readily to perverted abuse by parents, spouses, preachers, and others who feel themselves qualified to</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:501.91px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">express God’s wrath at human failing. This punishment can be physical or, more dangerously,</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:515.95px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">emotional. Having heard the tearful confessions of a teenager who is a serial offender against God’s</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:529.99px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">clear indictment against sexual promiscuity, what dutiful priest would be so remiss as not to whip the</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:544.03px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">fear of God into any such errant youth (while also releasing his libidinal tension)?</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:72.02px;top:559.99px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Security: People feel reassured when swaddled in the faith of their fathers. In times of trouble, people</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:574.03px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">long for the security of their infancy, when their believer-parents cradled them and taught them “As I</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:588.07px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">lay me down to sleep…”</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:72.02px;top:604.18px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Sex with children (clergy only, please!): Catholic priests, possibly because they are forbidden to marry,</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:618.22px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">repeatedly run afoul of social norms in their exuberance to ram the fear of God into young boys and</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:632.26px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">girls. Additionally, ages-long suppression of homosexuals has led naturally to the gravitation of persons</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:646.18px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">so inclined to the priesthood, where they can live out their fantasies while protected by the Church.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:660.22px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Mormon preachers are also allowed to express their love of God on underage girls completely legally,</span></div>

<div style="position:absolute;left:72.02px;top:67.20px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">sometimes even with the coercive encouragement of the child’s parents.  Leaders of cults also often find</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:81.26px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">this particular perk irresistible.</span></div>

<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:111.26px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">opposing argument, some people are simply unwilling to give their (obviously demonic) adversary the</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:125.30px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">satisfaction.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:72.02px;top:141.38px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Survival (~Community above): Persecuted religious minorities identify with their religion and believe</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:155.42px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">they must stick together to survive.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:72.02px;top:343.37px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Vanity: The church becomes “my team” and maybe even has a flag, to which one can feel a form of</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:357.41px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">“patriotism.”</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:72.02px;top:373.49px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">These reasons are potent by themselves, but when used in combination, they are nearly insurmountable</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:387.53px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">for an adult, much less a child.</span></div>

<div style="position:absolute;left:280.61px;top:67.20px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">False Prophets</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:72.02px;top:81.26px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">How do we know a false prophet?</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:109.10px;top:95.30px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">‘When a prophet speaketh in the name of the LORD, if the thing follow not, nor come to</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:116.18px;top:109.34px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">pass, that is the thing which the LORD hath not spoken, but the prophet hath spoken it</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:174.02px;top:123.38px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">presumptuously: thou shalt not be afraid of him.’  (Deu 18:22)</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:72.02px;top:139.34px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">Obviously all those who have hitherto predicted the end of the world have been wrong, and are</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:153.38px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">therefore, by the biblical definition, false prophets. It’s an impressive list. Notice how much</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:167.42px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">more frequent they have become recently. The date given is that of the predicted End.</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:72.02px;top:183.38px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">~50 CE Jesus, “And he said unto them, Verily I say unto you, That there be some of them that stand</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:197.42px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">here, which shall not taste of death, till they have seen the kingdom of God come with power.” (Mark</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:211.46px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">9:1)</span></div>

<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:241.58px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">66-70 in Judea as the final end-time battle which would bring about the arrival of the Messiah. By the</span></div>
<div style="position:absolute;left:81.02px;top:255.65px" class="cls_003"><span class="cls_003">authority of High Priest Simon, coins were minted declaring the redemption of Israel.</span></div>
